India-Japan Trade Negotiations: British Reply to Japan 58

Refusal to Grant India Diplomatic Power

Reason: To Promote Independence

(Tokyo) Regarding the India-Japan negotiations, the Japanese government repeatedly requested that the British government grant the Indian government diplomatic power. The British government has deeply studied the purpose of this proposal put forward by Japan and believes that the Japanese side intends to use this as an opportunity to help promote India's independence. Foreign Minister Simon then replied to Ambassador Matsudaira, rejecting this proposal. The main points of the British reply are as follows: ㈠ The Indian government has special significance in the British Constitution, and the United Kingdom cannot grant it independent diplomatic negotiating power. ㈡ The Indian independence movement is becoming increasingly fierce and cannot be used as a temporary convenience to promote the independence trend. If independent negotiating power is granted, the government must be responsible to the parliament and be questioned by it. ㈢ The British government will, within the scope of possibility, not create difficulties in the results of the Japan-India contact and will not fundamentally change the original proposal. (Hualian dispatch, 29th)

(Tokyo) According to an official announcement released here today, Japan previously asked the United Kingdom whether it would grant full power to the Indian delegation to the Japan-India Commercial Conference in Shimla. Now, according to an informal reply, for technical reasons, the United Kingdom cannot grant the Indian representatives the power to conduct diplomatic negotiations, and it is feared that this move will encourage the excitement of Indians seeking independence. However, the British government is willing to guarantee that the British government does not want to make fundamental changes to any commercial agreements concluded between Japan and India. The main idea of the reply was conveyed by Ambassador Matsudaira in the UK to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. (Reuters dispatch, 29th)

East Africa Rejects Japanese Goods 59

Japan Believes Britain is Using Means to Reject Japanese Goods

(Tokyo) According to a report from Consul Kuwajima in Mombasa (British territory in Africa) to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, British merchants in the area have recently felt threatened due to the entry and exit of Japanese goods. On the 25th, the Joint General Assembly of the East African Chamber of Commerce resolved to revise the Congo Treaty and the League of Nations Mandate Terms, because these two items restrict the freedom of East Africa's finance and economy, making it impossible for the United Kingdom to implement its special privileges, and there is a risk of promoting the entry and exit of Japanese merchants and immigrants. The so-called Congo Treaty refers to the commercial treaty based on the most-favored-nation treatment signed between the colonies in the Congo Basin and Japan and major European powers. The League of Nations Mandate Terms recognize the right of League of Nations member states to have most-favored-nation treatment in the area. The rejection of Japanese goods movement in Mombasa is, according to the observation of the Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs, a means by which the British reject Japanese goods, and its trend is extremely noteworthy. Italian-Hungarian Talks Successful 76

Rome, July 28 (Havas) Hungarian Prime Minister General Gömbös told representatives of the foreign press, "The purpose of my visit to Italy is to study various issues concerning the European situation with Italian Prime Minister Mussolini. As a result of my talks with Mussolini, the Italian and Hungarian governments are very pleased that we have a consensus on various economic and political issues."

Budapest, July 28 (National News) The newspapers in the Hungarian capital have thoroughly reported on the talks between Hungarian Prime Minister Gömbös and Mussolini in Italy, praising the closeness of their views and the success of the results, and stating that the revision of the treaty that the Hungarian government hopes for is a foregone conclusion.

The newspapers all stated that Italian public opinion has expressed full support for the revision of the treaty, and French public opinion is also gradually moving towards coordination.

Berlin, July 28 (National News) The Berliner Tageblatt recently published a detailed report on the results of Hungarian Prime Minister Gömbös's visit to Italy. Its conclusion is that the signing of the Four-Power Pact has not only not harmed the relations between Italy and Hungary but has also increased the friendship between the two countries because Italy has not abandoned its long-standing claim to find a way for Hungary to revise the peace treaty after signing the pact. Furthermore, an understanding has been reached between Italy and Hungary regarding the Danube River basin issue. On the one hand, Hungary supports Italy's various attempts in the Danube River, and Italy recognizes Hungary's economic relations with the Danube River basin. Italian Prime Minister Mussolini will continue to strive to obtain the consent of the other three countries within the Four-Power Pact to resolve the Danube River and Balkan issues. In addition, ways to increase the economic relations between Italy and Hungary have also been established. However, the countries of the Little Entente have apparently been greatly disturbed by the Hungarian Prime Minister's visit to Italy this time, and the opposition arguments made by Romanian Minister of Justice Bobuvisy can also represent a glimpse of the current emotions of the countries of the Little Entente. Bobuvisy recently published a speech stating that since a Four-Power Pact has been signed, all talk of treaty revision has been abandoned for ten years, but if this matter is brought up again, it should first be stated that the so-called treaty revision is purely a matter of power and that revision means war.

Russia and Spain Restore Diplomatic Relations 77

Foreign Ministers Exchange Notes

Moscow, July 28 (TASS) The Soviet Union and Spain have exchanged notes and formally restored diplomatic relations, which were broken after the establishment of the Soviet Union in 1917. Spanish Foreign Minister Los Rios had sent a letter to Litvinov, stating that the Spanish government had recognized the Soviet government in fact and in law. Soviet Deputy Foreign Minister Krestinsky, in reply to this note, said that the Soviet Union, motivated by a solid and universal desire for peace and to restore friendly relations between the Soviet Union and Spain, had recognized the government of the Spanish Republic in fact and in law as the only legitimate and powerful government in Spain. Krestinsky also stated in his reply that the Soviet government is now prepared to immediately exchange ambassadors and conduct negotiations to conclude a commercial treaty as the basis for the development of commercial relations between the Soviet Union and Spain.

Records of the Great Academic Exploration of Manchuria and Mongolia (3) (Translated from Osaka Asahi Shimbun) 83

Rehe is rich in natural resources, surpassing all other provinces in Manchuria and Mongolia. However, due to the lack of detailed surveys, it is difficult to know the extent of its mineral deposits. Upon examination, the entire area of Rehe is mostly mountainous. According to geological classification, it can be divided into mountainous zones, plateau zones, and desert zones. Each of these zones has its own geological characteristics. The mountainous zone is composed of gneiss, Paleozoic strata, Mesozoic strata, and Tertiary strata, followed by igneous rocks such as granite, basalt, quartz trachyte, and porphyry. The plateau zone belongs to the Quaternary strata and the widely distributed alluvial loess layer. The desert zone has porphyry outcrops. Gneiss, including hornblende gneiss, biotite gneiss, augen gneiss, quartz gneiss, and lamprophyre, is widely distributed from the Guoding Mountains, the Daqing Mountains, to the southwest of Jinzhou, occupying a vast area especially from the vicinity of Baoguo Temple to Jianchang. The Paleozoic strata are composed of argillite, sandstone, hard sandstone, limestone, and tuff. In parts of the Daqing Mountains and various locations in the Phoenix Mountains, as well as near Chengde and Chaoyang, carbonaceous rocks are exposed in the upper layers. The direction of these strata generally extends eastward from 30 to 60 degrees north, with a dip of 50 to 60 degrees to the southeast, penetrating granite, porphyry, and basalt. The Mesozoic strata consist of thick layers of porphyry, tuff, agglomerate, and angular breccia, containing a carbonaceous layer in the upper Jurassic period, overlying the irregular Paleozoic strata. The direction of the strata extends from northeast to southwest, distributed in Qinghebianmen, Jinzhou, Jianchang, Xinqiu, Yuejiagou, Chaoyang, Dachengzi, and the Binggou coalfield. The Tertiary strata are composed of ocher sandstone, breccia, shale, and tuff, containing quartz trachyte, basalt, and andesite, distributed in Xitumote, Jinchanggou Liang, Chaoyang, and Dongtumote, Xinlitu. The main component of the Quaternary is the alluvial loess layer, which is widely distributed. In low-lying areas, yellowish-brown rocks accumulate everywhere, with a thickness of 20 to 30 to 130 feet. The extent of mineral resources in Rehe Province is currently difficult to determine. However, the vast coal seams of the Middle Ages in the Songling Mountains and the Paleozoic strata of the Yinshan Mountains, containing gold and silver, have long been established. Other minerals such as copper, iron, lead, crude oil, asbestos, soda, glass stone, sulfur, silica, crystal, gems, fluorite, salt, and limestone are abundantly buried everywhere. The largest product is bituminous coal, extending from Fuxin through Chaoyang to Jinxi County, as well as the main and tributary basins of the Laohe River, including Fengning and Pingquan counties, all of which are inexhaustible mineral veins. Gold and placer gold are abundant in the main and tributary basins of the Luan River, including Fengning, Chengde, Luanping, and Longhua counties, and the main tributary basins of the Laohe River and its tributary Yingjin River, including Chaoyang and Lingyuan counties. The products from the lakes and marshes are supplied to Mongolian tribes and to the border regions of Heilongjiang, Hebei, Gansu, and Shanxi. The above refers to the area south of the Xilamulun River. As for the area north of the Xilamulun River, the useful mineral deposits are even richer but have not yet been mined. In other words, the minerals stored in the basin of the Laohe River, a tributary of the Xilamulun River, and the basin of the Yingjin River, a tributary of the Xilamulun River (i.e., in the main stream of the Xilamulun River and its northern regions).

The most prominent gold mines are in the Daheishan Mountains of Jinchanggou Liang, and the coal mines are centered in Chaoyang, extending from Fuxin County to the Kalaqin Left Banner, and centered in Chifeng, extending northeast to southwest, which are called mineral-producing zones. Other promising areas have not yet been investigated and are unknown. In the future, all depends on our efforts, and we should be able to discover them one by one.

In terms of geography, according to Tada Fumio, no geographers have thoroughly investigated the Rehe region. Previously, Percy Eyer of England, Merendorff of Germany, Dr. Ogawa Takuji of Japan, and recently Chertan of France, as well as Sven Hedin, a Swede who explored Mongolia, Central Asia, and Tibet, failed to obtain a complete picture. Therefore, in geography, Rehe is called a "dark zone." However, the important issues of this region have always been considered inconceivable by explorers and scholars from various countries. From the perspective of physical geography, this area is the intermediate mountainous zone between the flat Mongolian plateau, the low-lying northern part of China, and the Manchurian plains. On the Mongolian plateau, there are several stepped peneplains, and there is also a low-lying peneplain on the Liaodong Peninsula. How these are expressed and contrasted in this transitional zone is a major research question. From the perspective of climate, the Rehe region is a transitional zone between the arid desert region and the rainy, mild, and hot region. Therefore, research from a biogeographical perspective is quite interesting. As for human geography, this region was originally the border area between the Han, Mongolian, and Manchu ethnic groups. We should investigate the rise and fall of the distribution of their forces. The nomadic peoples living in the dry areas from the Caspian Sea to the Gobi Desert are very different from the agricultural peoples surrounding the monsoon region of Southeast Asia. How the cultures of these two peoples harmonize in the bordering area and form a cultural landscape is a matter for research. Therefore, judgment can only be made after our investigation and research. In summary, the importance of Manchurian and Mongolian resources to Japan is self-evident. At present, our country (Japan) has shifted from an agrarianism to an industrial nation. However, Japan's industrialization, in terms of technology and capital, is no longer a problem. The only obstacle is the lack of raw materials. Most of the important industrial raw materials produced in Japan, except for raw silk, are insufficient. Now, to seek raw material supplies in a safe area, we rely entirely on the Asian continent. In particular, from the perspective of defense in Manchuria and Mongolia, it is the key to the proper propagation of the Imperial Way. Other economic issues such as population and food issues, industrial raw material issues, and property market issues are related to Japan's survival. It is a region that supplies the resources that the Empire lacks. Therefore, the dispatch of this scientific survey team demonstrates the importance of our country's (Japan's) mission.

The above is translated from the special edition of the Osaka Asahi Shimbun dated July 23rd, which was published on the day the survey team departed for the first time. As for the team's actual survey report, according to the schedule, the first step of the survey will begin between Beipiao and Chaoyang from August 5th to 10th. It is expected that the Asahi Shimbun will receive the report on the 13th or 14th, and our newspaper should be able to translate and publish it successively on the 16th and 17th. The reporter has endless thoughts writing this. Our country has been in turmoil for more than twenty years, and there has been no peaceful year. The rulers have no time to develop resources, coupled with a lack of talent, resulting in the mysterious territories being given away, which is very regrettable.

X X X X

Inspection Report of Jiangxi, Anhui, Hunan, and Hubei by Our Newspaper's Special Correspondent Ren An 84

Linchuan as a Military Center

Special dispatch from Linchuan: Linchuan, formerly known as Fuzhou, has convenient transportation and fertile land, and is one of the best counties in Jiangxi Province. However, since the county borders bandit areas, it has become the center of the Central Route Bandit Suppression Military. The passage of bandit suppression troops, the transport of ammunition and salaries to the front lines of Yihuang, Le'an, Chongren, Huangpi, Nanfeng, and Nancheng, all depend on this. Refugees from bandit areas also mostly gather here. The population in the city is increasing day by day, and the streets are also quite bustling. However, the business of the shops feels deserted, because the purchasing power of the general public is low. The Eighth Provincial Middle School, other government offices, and spacious private residences are also mostly borrowed by the stationed troops. The city's defensive works are constantly being repaired. Pedestrians are strictly checked. The search for bandits and their parties happens almost every day. The tension of bandit suppression is more severe than in Nanchang.

According to County Magistrate Xia of this county, the bandit suppression military has been going on for five years. The local burden has long exhausted its resources. Even taking the issue of yicha (corvée labor) as an example, in addition to the countless dispatches made earlier, in the past two weeks alone, another thousand people have been dispatched. The county government has no way to scrape together resources, so it has to recruit with county rewards. Those who can recruit thirty laborers are appointed as platoon leaders with a monthly salary of twenty yuan. Those who can recruit one hundred and twenty laborers are promoted to company commanders with a monthly salary of thirty yuan. Generally, those who are wealthy and have leadership desires, and

Page 10

Have some military experience come out to call for them and encourage them to take charge. The rice straw within thirty miles of the city has long been used up for military purposes. The desire for a stalk is as precious as wisdom. However, every time the troops set off, the paper required is still like snowflakes, saying that it is urgently needed and must be obeyed, or that it concerns bandit suppression and must not be delayed. Other temporary requisitions of various donations and taxes mostly gain the favor of the government but lose the hearts of the people, and are particularly thorny to comply with. Fortunately, the baojia system in the county is becoming more and more perfect, and the training of the Bao Wei Tuan (local defense corps) is effective, which can fulfill the responsibility of maintaining local security. The telephone network in each village and town has been completed, so there is no need to worry about a lack of response in case of a bandit alarm, etc.

The refugees gathered here are all from bandit areas and near bandit areas (war zones between soldiers and bandits), such as Jinxi, Chongren, Le'an, and other eight counties. According to the surveys of the county and township associations, there are a total of five thousand. Zhou Zuofu, the Special Commissioner of the Seventh Administrative Inspectorate District of Jiangxi Province, obtained a relief fund of five thousand yuan from Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, and distributed it by roll call in the public sports field, one yuan per person, and gave a small photo of Chiang Kai-shek. It took eight days to complete the matter. The refugees' clothes are mostly silk, and many of the old women wear large-edged and large-rolled, antique costumes, which almost make one suspect that they are not modern people, not genuine refugees. However, upon detailed inquiry, none of them had not abandoned their property and fields. It is particularly sad. As for the lower middle class, even if they want to escape, they do not have the strength. If they do not become bandits, they will be slaughtered, and their suffering is even more unimaginable. It is heard that after the distribution of relief, many refugees have returned to their hometowns one after another.

I visited a friend at headquarters and asked about the bandit situation. He provided a report from a certain regimental commander on the Yihuang defense line, which discussed the strengths and weaknesses of the bandits in detail. The general meaning is as follows: The bandits have three advantages: (1) The officers and soldiers all have political consciousness, so they can enforce strict military discipline and command as desired. They once peered at their battle line with a telescope and saw that even in the trenches, they would occasionally hold meetings and speeches. It can be seen that the movement of military politicization, even in wartime, is not relaxed. (2) They pay attention to propaganda. The bandits are in a favorable position, and are anesthetized by propaganda every day, and are unrepentant until death. However, they also print various slogans on paper and send them with the wind, or write them on wooden boards and float them downstream, in order to communize the good people and soldiers. (3) They are calm in battle. If the bandits take a defensive position, no matter how the National Army attacks, they will not easily counterattack, making it difficult to discern their weaknesses. Their shortcomings are not only one. However, the lack of supplies may be their fatal injury. Since the implementation of the red zone blockade policy, every ounce of salt has now risen to two yuan, and one sheng (pint) of rice is three yuan, making life extremely difficult. The clothes are also mostly tattered, etc. Later, my friend added that the number of bandit soldiers and officers who have surrendered and been admitted to the 感化院 (rehabilitation center) set up by the headquarters has reached more than five hundred. The lack of supplies on the bandit side is also a reason for the dispersal of the masses.

According to a cooperative investigator, the rural economic situation here has already shown a small-scale peasant economy centered on semi-tenant farmers. Income cannot cover expenses, and they mostly rely on cow-rolling (borrowing and pawning to survive), barely maintaining their lives. The need for relief is urgent. However, when we (the investigator refers to himself) went to promote the organization of cooperatives in order to restore rural prosperity, the general farmers were suspicious and often used the excuse that setting up another organization in the countryside would require an expense to politely decline. Therefore, although the call for promoting the organization of cooperatives has been sung for a long time, only seven have been formally established in practice. (July 20)

Past Events of the Fall of Nancheng 85

Special dispatch from Nancheng: Going south from Linchuan, one gradually enters the bandit area. Nancheng and Nanfeng were once captured by bandits. Although they have now been recovered and heavily garrisoned, there are guerrilla forces of bandits who appear from time to time in the countryside more than five miles outside the city. Therefore, highway bridges and telegraph poles along the road are often burned, and car robbery is especially common. The military authorities are advocating the construction of bridges and碉樓 (fortified watchtowers) to maintain transportation, which will soon be put into practice.

I departed from Linchuan in the morning and arrived in Nancheng at noon. Along the way, many tall pine trees were planted on the slopes, and the early rice in the paddy fields was already ripe, with golden clouds as far as the eye could see. Farmers were busy harvesting. The car entered the county's警戒線 (perimeter security line), and both soldiers and civilians were subject to interrogation. The streets and alleys passed after getting off the car were mostly winding paths due to military obstacles. The walls on both sides were not only covered with slogans, but also had gun holes dug into them, leaving no gaps. Upon entering the city, one was inspected again, and government employees had to show their passports, and merchants had to show their badges. If they were villagers coming to the city to catch the market, in addition to wearing a 良民證章 (good citizen badge) on their chest, they also had to obtain a 通行路單 (pass) from the Baojia chief every day, with the following rules:

(1) This pass is limited to one person for one use (not restricting the number of uses, but the usage time is limited to one day). After the expiration, it must still be returned to the Bao chief for verification. (2) This pass is not allowed to be lent to others or lost, otherwise it will be reported to the county magistrate and treated as collusion with bandits. (3) This pass is valid within the county's jurisdiction and within twenty li (about six miles) of neighboring counties. (4) When people request a pass, they must pay one copper coin to the Bao chief as a paper and printing fee, but they must not overcharge or underpay.

From these pass rules, it can be seen that people near the bandit areas not only cannot move freely, but also occasionally have suspicions of colluding with bandits if they are not careful. Therefore, the general villagers, except for those who have to sell firewood in exchange for oil, salt, and groceries, otherwise they all regard entering the city as a fearsome thing. For example, if they want to sell pig manure, they would usually drive the pig into the city to earn a high price. At this time, they would only post a notice in the village, writing "So-and-so will slaughter a pig on such-and-such day, and is willing to sell it by the catty at a low price," etc. Those villagers who have wanted meat for a long time will then go to share it. Other miscellaneous grains and groceries are also mostly traded in this way. Also, although the pass only stipulates that one copper coin should be paid, in reality, two or even four coins are often collected. As for the so-called good citizen badge, it is a square inch of white cloth with the name, age, and address written on it, and stamped with a Baojia seal. Each badge costs four to five hundred cash, and it is especially troublesome to lose.

The streets in the city are mostly narrow, and even the store eaves on both sides are only two or three feet apart. The light is insufficient, and the air is especially difficult to breathe. The pedestrians are bustling and continuous, and most of them are refugees and soldiers. Notices for selling good houses and seeking to sell good fields are often seen on the streets and alleys.

I took the opportunity to visit the county government and was received by a certain section chief. According to him, the bandits captured the city for five days the year before last, forcing the Chamber of Commerce to raise funds and prepare food, and using local ruffians to search wealthy families for countless items of clothing, which were arbitrarily distributed on the Tianyi Mountain stage. If the people under the stage did not accept them, they would shout loudly, "Are you a capitalist?" Later, when they saw the iron birds (airplanes) flying, they scattered like birds and beasts. The fields in the semi-bandit area (i.e., the war zone between soldiers and bandits) have all been abandoned, and the rest can be cultivated as usual. It is heard that the arable land in the bandit area was initially distributed based on the population and the area of the bandits. Later, due to the small number of people and the large amount of land, production was encouraged. A method of collecting 20 catties out of every 100 catties of grain was used to concentrate food. Due to economic panic, three public bonds of 5 jiao (0.5 yuan), 1 yuan, and 1.5 yuan were issued. People between the ages of 16 and 35 all have the obligation to join the Red Army and 赤衛隊 (red guards). The masses mostly dare to be angry but dare not speak out, hoping that the National Army will advance and suppress them to relieve their suffering. Later, I asked him to introduce me to the Nanfeng government. He pointed to the high mountains twenty li (about six miles) away and said, "The car is likely to be robbed by bandits near this mountain. The situation in Nanfeng is roughly the same as here. If there is no important business, it is not necessary to go."

The money and grain taxes in this area, in addition to the regular and supplementary tax silver dollars, increase year by year, and there are also 公政捐 (public administration donations), 伕差捐 (corvée labor donations), 禾草捐 (rice straw donations), 保甲捐 (baojia donations), and 飛機測量捐 (airplane surveying donations), etc. The fields destroyed and occupied by the highway and county roads, which should be exempt from grain tax, have not been allowed, and the suffering they have endured is unspeakable. (July 25)

Bird's-Eye View of Bandit Suppression in Hubei Province 86

Eastern Hubei: Capturing Three Bandit Nests and Killing a Bandit Division Commander

Western Hubei: The Second Phase of General Suppression Surrounded and Attacked Wuyang Pass

Southern Hubei: Jiangxi Bandits Retreat and Two Divisions Led by Guo and Rong Jointly Suppress

Communication from Hankou: Since the large-scale mobilization of the bandit suppression army in Hubei Province, progress has been rapid. The forces of Kuang Jixun, He Long, Kong Hechong, etc., are on the verge of collapse again. Here is a comprehensive summary of the bandit suppression situation in various aspects:

Eastern Hubei 87

The bandits in Eastern Hubei include the pseudo Twenty-fourth, Twenty-fifth, Twenty-eighth Armies, and various guerrilla forces, separately led by pseudo army commanders Liao Rongkun, Shen Zemin, and Lü Huanxian, all under the banner of Kuang Jixun. However, there has been no confirmed report on whether Kuang is in the army. The occupied bandit area, in addition to parts of Huangma and Luotian counties in Hubei Province, also extends to southern Henan and western Anhui. The Soviet government of the border area of the three provinces of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui is located in Guojiahe, with Qiliping and Dushuihe as its important gateways. After Liu Zhenhua completed the deployment of various forces, he ordered a general suppression. The bandits knew they were no match, and on one hand, they stubbornly resisted by defending strategic locations, and on the other hand, they split up and fled. The main force of the Twenty-fifth Army, the 73rd and 74th Divisions, has been defeated by the troops sent by Liu. A pseudo division commander was killed on the spot, and countless bandits were killed. The Liang Guanying unit of the Twenty-fifth Route Army also came into contact with the main force of the bandits and fought fiercely for two days and nights. On the 26th, they recovered Dushuihe. On the 28th, they took advantage of the victory and occupied Guojiahe, destroying the pseudo government. The remnants of this force have now fled to Qiliping, and Liang's unit is chasing and suppressing them. One force in the Macheng area, about several thousand people, previously fled to Nanliuhe and Baishahe in the southern township of Lihuang, and some remained in Futianhe in Mashu. Recently, the Hao Mengling unit of the Fifty-fourth Division fought fiercely and captured the Futianhe bandit nest. The bandits who fled to Henan attempted to rescue them, so they returned from Nanliuhe and Baishahe to spy on Macheng and Luotian. Upon hearing the report, Liu Zhenhua ordered the entire Shangguan Yunxiang of the Forty-seventh Division to be transferred to Songziguan and Shengjiabao to prevent the bandits from going south. The headquarters of the division was moved to Luotian County to facilitate command. As for the Manchu conference convened by Liu, it was held in Manchu on the 28th. A precise study on the suppression and aftermath of the bandits in Eastern Hubei is being conducted. The conference is scheduled for three days and will be closed on the 30th.

Western Hubei 88

The He bandits in Western Hubei have been entrenched in the Five Crane Mountains for a long time. The government army cannot drive straight in due to the difficulty of transporting supplies. However, precisely because the mountain paths are rugged, there is no way for the bandits to transport supplies either, and the blockade policy has achieved significant results. Xu Yuanquan, the Commander-in-Chief of Bandit Suppression in the Hubei-Hunan Border Region, who was ordered to supervise the suppression, officially took office on the 20th. After discussing with He Chengzun, the Director of the Pacification Affairs, he ordered a general suppression. Zhang Gang, the commander of the security team, and Jiang Zuojun, the commander of the New Third Brigade, served as vanguards, and first captured the Crane Peak bandit nest. The first phase of the suppression plan was completed. Soon after, the key points of Ximaping, Shadaoping, Hongtuxi, and Shihuiyao were successively occupied. The second phase of the suppression plan is now being implemented, surrounding and attacking the Wuyang Pass bandit nest. This place is where the He bandits are stationed in person, and their strength is relatively abundant. They are expected to hold on firmly. Xu has added the entire Pan Shanzhai brigade to the front line, setting a three-day deadline to recover the pass. Xu himself will go to Changyang on the 29th to supervise the army and telegraph the Sichuan and Hunan armies to guard the key points to prevent them from fleeing far.

Southern Hubei 89

The remnants of the Kong bandits in Southern Hubei previously fled to the Xiutong area on the border of Jiangxi. Recently, taking advantage of the National Army's troop transfer, a part has fled into Hubei, and there are traces of red bandits in the Taizimiao, Fenghuangshan, and Fushou districts of Yangxin County, and they are very rampant. People are mostly fleeing to Qichun, where they are being received by Gu Renfa, the Special Commissioner of the Third Administrative Inspectorate District. Upon receiving the report, the Pacification Office telegraphed Guo Rudong, the commander of the Twenty-sixth Division, and Rong Jingfang, the commander of the Eighty-second Division, to send troops to jointly suppress them. (July 28)

Liu Xiang's Telegram to Wang Jingwei and Chiang Kai-shek on Bandit Suppression Opinions 90

The Three Major Procedures for Bandit Suppression and Pacification of Sichuan

Reasons for Past Failures in Bandit Suppression

Politics Should Proceed Slowly During Military Times

Chongqing Correspondence: Liu Xiang, Commander-in-Chief of Bandit Suppression in Sichuan, sent a telegram to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek and President Wang Jingwei of the National Government on the 23rd, outlining the procedures for bandit suppression and methods for managing the various armies. The following is an excerpt: "Yesterday, I received your order, specially appointing Xiang as Commander-in-Chief of Bandit Suppression in Sichuan, with all the armies in Sichuan under my command. I also received the issued letter of appointment and official seals, etc. Upon receiving this order, I was deeply apprehensive. Considering my limited abilities, how can I bear such a great responsibility? Xiang has been managing the army in Sichuan for many years and has some experience in suppressing communists and bandits. Regardless of my limitations, I humbly offer my humble opinion for your wise consideration. I believe that when discussing bandit suppression and pacification of Sichuan today, there should be clear procedures and distinctions that must not be confused. First, manage the various armies, unify their will, eliminate obstacles, and jointly stabilize the situation in Sichuan. Second, the armies should be sincerely and closely organized, assigned tasks, and eliminate the Red bandits. Third, unify the Sichuan administration and strive for construction. The above three points are necessary stages with fixed methods. If they are not clear or if the order is reversed, bandit suppression will actually support the bandits, and suppressing communism will instead create communism. The past is clear, and no one can violate this principle. Taking the Red bandits in northern Sichuan as an example, the various units have been suppressing them for more than half a year. Statistics show that the Yang, Tian, and Liu armies have more than ten brigades in total. They have burdened Sichuan and wasted resources, but they have not harmed the Red bandits in the slightest. Instead, they have been taken advantage of by the bandits, and Tongjiang and Bazhong have fallen again, which cannot be salvaged. The reasons for the failure can be stated as follows: (1) The various units defended against the bandits in their respective areas without close organization; (2) There was no appropriate political deployment, and there was no sufficient preparation for weapons and supplies. In addition, Liu defended Deng, which affected Tian's unit, and the armies had divided loyalties and many concerns. Therefore, although there were many troops, only a few could actually be used. With such bandit suppression, how could it not be suppressed by the bandits? According to recent intelligence, the bandits and government troops were not always in close contact. Sometimes the distance between them was very far, with gaps of hundreds of miles. However, the bandits did not dare to approach, which shows that the bandits' situation is not as fierce as rumored. Only the government side has no means of providing supplies, and transportation is failing, so they are often taken advantage of by the bandits, resulting in endless disasters. Therefore, bandit suppression without a plan is actually welcomed by the bandits, and its harm is far greater than not suppressing them at all. Xiang was born and raised in Sichuan, where his ancestors' graves are located. He respects and cherishes his homeland, and I believe that I am second to none. If there is a shortcut to take, I would have done my best to take it. However, in reality, there are many constraints that need to be eliminated. It seems roundabout, but it is not my intention. The situation in Sichuan is such that it cannot be delayed. I have decided to follow the above-mentioned procedures and proceed in earnest. In the shortest possible time, I will manage the various armies, promote their joint progress, and eliminate the banditry. Everything will be easily resolved. If it takes too long and there is no success, then I ask to be punished for the crime of misleading the country, to punish one to warn a hundred, starting with myself. However, at this time of managing the Sichuan army and eliminating obstacles, there are many doubts and tremors, and there are many words of speculation. I hope that you will thoroughly investigate and resolve the concerns. If you do not bother the eyes and ears of the common people and hastily patch things up, dealing with them in a piecemeal manner, then you are deceiving yourself and others, seeking temporary praise, and leaving great trouble for the future. Although Xiang is ignorant and incompetent, I dare not accept such an order. Furthermore, during military operations, it is most important to have a unified will. Political issues should be postponed for now. Issues such as organizing the provincial government and allocating powers are very important, but if they are raised now, they will only shake the will and divide the various units. This should be noted. Xiang has received special treatment, entrusted with full authority to suppress bandits and pacify Sichuan. I am always fearful and dare not claim credit. At the beginning of this assignment, I have to comprehensively consider the overall situation and carefully consider it. I dare not disobey your orders or delay the time, nor can I tolerate raising problems and repeating the mistakes of the past. Before reporting the new appointment, I am extremely worried and can only lay out my honest opinion, hoping that you will understand my foolish sincerity and secretly give me your guidance. I am in utmost fear and await your orders."

Establishment Period of the 19th Route Army Supplementary Division 91

All Units Have Arrived in the Province for Reorganization

The Brigade and Regiment Commanders Have Also Been Appointed

Fuzhou Correspondence: After the 19th Route Army's two columns supporting Rehe returned to their garrison, commanders Zhang Yan and Tan Qixiu were both promoted from Chief Commanders to Division Commanders. Zhang was appointed to the 49th Division and took office in Yongding a few days ago. Tan was appointed to the Supplementary Division and flew to the province a few days ago to discuss the division's reorganization plan with the Pacification Headquarters. It has been decided to combine the three regiments of the 19th Route Army Supplementary Brigade currently stationed downstream in Haicheng and Tong'an, the two regiments of the Security Brigade stationed in the provincial capital Xixiang, and the 2nd Special Service Regiment of the 19th Route Army stationed upstream in Minqing and Yongtai into one division. In addition to Tan Qixiu serving as Division Commander and concurrently Commander of the 1st Brigade, Chen Wei-yuan, Commander of the 2nd Security Brigade, will serve as Deputy Division Commander, Xiao Zu, Chief of Staff of the Supplementary Brigade Headquarters, will serve as Chief of Staff of the Division Headquarters, and Situ Fei, Commander of the 2nd Special Service Regiment, will serve as Commander of the 2nd Brigade. As for the Deputy Brigade Commander and Regiment Commander candidates, Tan and the Pacification Headquarters are currently discussing them, and they will likely be selected from the current regiment commanders of the Supplementary and Security Brigades and the battalion commanders of the Special Service Regiment. The Division Headquarters has selected the Liu Guanxiong family ancestral hall in Dusi Lane in the city, and Xiao Zu is supervising personnel to move in for office work and is starting to handle the reorganization matters. The upstream and downstream troops have been continuously arriving in the province in recent days and are stationed in the City Defense Office, City God Temple, Faha Temple, and Xijian and Zhejiang Guildhall outside the West Gate. Tan Qixiu and Xiao Zu are going to inspect and verify them, with a deadline of the end of the month. A portion of the old and weak will be eliminated, and the vacancies will be filled by new Guangdong and Guangxi recruits recruited by the New Soldier Training Office of the Pacification Headquarters. It is rumored that the most soldiers will be eliminated from the Security Brigade. As for the establishment date, it is set for August 1st, and the division, brigade, and regiment commanders will simultaneously take their oaths of office. After the reorganization of the Security Brigade, the important officers of the Brigade Headquarters will be transferred to the Pacification Headquarters as staff officers and adjutants. As for the garrison locations of the entire division, in addition to leaving a portion to maintain security in the provincial capital, the rest are planned to be deployed to Gutian, Minqing, Yongtai, and other counties near the province to carry out bandit suppression. Jiaxing Madman Sets Fire, Dies in Flames 100

Zhang Shijun, who lived in Tanghui Town, about two miles outside the north gate of Jiaxing, became insane because his wife had an affair with Wu Haoran, the former director of the town's public security sub-bureau. When Wu left his post, his wife went with him. Zhang Shijun's madness worsened. At about 9:00 PM on the 28th, Zhang lit the mosquito net with a match, and the fire quickly spread to the house. The neighborhood firefighters arrived to put out the fire, but two rows of buildings in the Zhang family mansion had already been reduced to ashes. Several Shen families who rented the house were also affected. When the fire was raging, Zhang Shijun did not escape and was buried in the fire.

Changshu Opposes Taxing Base Without Grain, Turning it into Official Property 101

In the urban area of this county, housing bases have never been taxed, and the county government is currently carrying out a supplementary grain tax. However, the official property office recently asked the Ministry of Finance whether the base without grain can be regarded as official property. The Ministry of Finance has issued an instruction that the base without grain should all be regarded as official property. Therefore, the supplementary grain tax has been shelved. The price for the base should be paid to the official property office before the supplementary grain tax can be carried out. The people are overburdened and are strongly opposed to it.

Zhang Quanrong, 47 years old, who lived in Zhao Lane, suddenly suffered from real cholera the other day. He was sent to the Xilong Epidemic Hospital. No More Inspection of Antiquities in the Forbidden City 110

The Media will be invited to report the inspection process

The inspection of antiquities stored in the Forbidden City Museum has been going on for three days. The work stopped on the afternoon of the day before yesterday. Yesterday at around 11:00, the Temporary Supervisory Committee held a meeting. The supervisors Chen Rui (Executive Yuan), Huang Penghao (Military Committee), Liu Yunhang (Municipal Council), Zhou Ren (Academia Sinica), Ouyang Shu (Local Court) and others attended to discuss the issue of exposing the fur clothing to the sun. Because the Supervisory Committee is only in a supervisory position, the Forbidden City Museum is responsible for the exposure. At the meeting, Zhou Ren and Zhuang Shangyan, two standing committee members, were directly contacted by Ma Heng, the president of the museum. However, although the price of fur clothing is valuable, it has no cultural value, so it was marked for sale in Beijing. Also, the fur clothing in the Shanghai boxes is only damp, so it does not seem to be a very important issue whether it is exposed to the sun or not. It was immediately decided that the inspection of antiquities was decided to come to an end, and no more inspections will be held in the future. Supervisors Chen Rui and Huang Penghao returned to Beijing yesterday to report everything. The Forbidden City Museum plans to invite news reporters in the near future to report all inspection information in detail so that people in the community can be fully informed of the inspection process.

Yang Dezhao Talks About Guangdong Affairs 111

France's Occupation of Small Islands in Southern Hainan, Guangdong Has Begun Research

Guangdong's Advance is Slow Due to the Suppression of Remnant Bandits

According to the National News Agency, Mr. Yang Dezhao, representative of Chen Jitang of Guangdong Province, arrived in Shanghai the night before yesterday. Yesterday, reporters met with Mr. Yang and asked about the suppression of bandits in Guangdong Province and France's occupation of nine small islands in southern Hainan. According to his answer, before I left Guangdong, I heard that Guangdong had already begun to study the issue of France's occupation of the nine islands, but how to deal with it after the research is unknown. Now, after reading the newspaper, I learned that the central government will send a warship from the Ministry of Navy to investigate. I believe that after the investigation, the reason for this will be clear. As for the military suppression of bandits, Guangdong Province has always had financial difficulties. In addition, overseas Chinese businessmen have been depressed in recent years and have been forced to return to the country, which is increasing. Therefore, it is becoming more and more exhausted. The military is progressing smoothly, but for the fundamental plan of the Guangdong army, for every city it conquers, it must build strong fortifications on one side, and the people's autonomy and transportation construction must be carried out simultaneously. Also, as far as food is concerned, the farmland has long been barren wherever the bandits have set foot, and it is impossible to cultivate it in a short time. Moreover, Guangdong rice is not enough to feed itself. Now, after the disaster caused by bandits, the price of rice has been soaring. All military food is purchased from Nanxiong and Shantou and transported for relief. Although the other Guangdong army has advanced to Ganzhou, there are still scattered bandits in Anyuan and Xunwu. With these various reasons, for the sake of fundamental suppression, Guangdong's advance seems to be a bit slow. Especially the transportation relationship is very large. The highway from Nanxiong to Ganzhou will be completed soon. At the same time, other five or six main lines are also being actively carried out. Mr. Chen Zhenru, I visited Hong Kong twice, but due to time constraints, I did not visit. However, Chen is still in Hong Kong. I will stay in Shanghai for three or four days, and then go to Beijing first, and then go to Lushan to visit Chairman Chiang to report everything.

Yu Hongjun Talks About the West Shanghai Power Supply Problem 112

Based on the Principle of Not Damaging Sovereignty

Both Sides are Exchanging Views

The electricity in the West Shanghai area of this city has always been supplied by the concession power company. The municipal government requested instructions from the central government on the matter, believing that it was related to Chinese sovereignty, so that it could carry out negotiations. The central government has determined 18 principles and ordered the municipal government to be informed. The municipal government immediately transferred the order to the municipal public utilities bureau to negotiate with the concession power company. A reporter from the Central News Agency asked Secretary-General Yu of the municipal government about the progress of the negotiations. According to him, the municipal government has ordered the municipal public utilities bureau to negotiate with the concession power company based on the central government's established guidelines. The principle is not to damage our country's sovereignty, but the concession power company has been operating the electricity business in West Shanghai for several years, so it is difficult to ask for any results at once. Currently, both sides are exchanging views.

Two Groups Welcome Aviators Chen Wenlin and Pan Dingxin 113

Report on the Flight from England Back to China

Aviator Chen Wenlin and aircraft manufacturer Pan Dingxin recently came to Shanghai from Xiamen on a Navy-built aircraft. The Deutera Verein and Tongji Alumni Association held a banquet to welcome Chen and Pan at the Fuxin Restaurant last night, as Chen and Pan had both studied in Germany. About fifty or sixty people attended. Huang Boqiao presided over the meeting, and Dr. You Pengxi reported on Chen and Pan's study of aircraft manufacturing in Germany. Then, Chen Wenlin was invited to speak about the flight from London back to China in 1928. Chen reported that when he flew back to China in 1928, he went through 14 countries and 34 stations, spending four to five hours at each station. He went through many dangers on the way. The first time he flew over the London Strait, the aircraft parts broke down and he returned to England for repairs. The second time, he was damaged in the desert in Persia and telegraphed to England to purchase aircraft parts. It took three weeks to get there, and the drinks were all transported from India. The food and lodging were unbearable. The third time, near Calcutta, he had to land in the Sha River due to oil leakage, and the fuselage overturned. He repaired it for many days. The fourth time, he was forced to land in Annam for some reason. After that, he flew safely to Xiamen. He originally intended to continue flying to Shanghai and Nanjing, but at that time, China's aviation was still very young. It took eight hours to fly from Xiamen to Shanghai, and the aircraft he was on could only hold seven hours of fuel, and there was no suitable airport along the way, so he could not continue flying. After I received the order from the Ministry of Navy to establish the Aviation Office in Xiamen, I worked hard to train flight and aircraft manufacturing talents. Fortunately, with the help of Mr. Pan Dingxin, I finally got my wish. The Jiangque aircraft, which I drove this time, except for the engine, is made of domestic products as much as possible and made by Chinese workers. However, I still feel that there are too few domestic products, and many parts have to be made with foreign products.

The Aircraft Association Notifies All Factories to Refuse to Accept English Letters from the Gongbu Bureau 114

Should be translated into Chinese and sent together to avoid misunderstandings

And pointed out two errors of the bureau

Regarding the Gongbu Bureau's warning to all factories, the Aircraft Association protested again yesterday and notified all members to refuse to accept foreign language letters from the Gongbu Bureau in the future. The details are as follows:

Public Concession Bureau's Error 115

After repeated warnings from the authorities of both the Public Concession and the French Concession to more than ten domestic goods factories, including Yi Yuan, Yi Sheng, Meiya, and China, each factory, fearing forced closure, has taken measures to improve automatically. The Machine Union believes that there are two errors in the warning letter from the Public Concession Bureau to the Yi Sheng Factory: (1) The chemical refining and grinding of rubber is essentially one type of work, but after investigation by the bureau members, the warning letter from the Public Concession Bureau actually separates them into two; (2) The shoe-hanging carts and freight carts in the rubber factory are completely different in nature. The pushing of shoe-hanging carts must not be forceful, as any force will damage the luster of the galoshes. However, after investigation by the bureau members, the warning letter from the Public Concession Bureau stated that efforts should be made to avoid working with iron tools on iron products or steel tools on steel products, and that the wheels of iron freight carts running on iron rails should not be made of iron or steel edges. Therefore, Chief Executive Cheng Shouchong, together with Yi Sheng Factory Director and Manager Tu Yanchen, questioned the Public Concession Bureau yesterday morning, and were received by He De Kui, who was in charge. He had no response to these two points and could only admit the errors.

Refusing to Accept English Letters 116

Yesterday, the Machine Union issued a notice to its members, stating: "Respectfully, since the Western taxpayers' association in the Public Concession unilaterally amended Article 34 of the Yangjingbang Regulations, forcing factories to obtain licenses from the Public Concession Bureau, hoping to seize the right to inspect Chinese factories, this association has repeatedly expressed its opposition. Unexpectedly, this time, the Public Concession Bureau, using Article 30 of the Yangjingbang Regulations as an excuse to 'prevent public danger,' ordered factories in the concession to stop work and relocate, which directly affects the economy and development of factories and the livelihoods of laborers, and indirectly affects the peace and order of society. This association has convened a temporary meeting to jointly devise countermeasures, and has submitted requests to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce of the municipal government and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for instructions, and requested that protests be lodged. At the same time, fearing that factories in the concession would obtain licenses from the Public Concession Bureau and cede sovereignty, we published declarations in the newspapers and, for the sake of public safety, assisted the Public Concession Bureau in providing as much guidance as possible on factory improvements to eliminate hidden dangers and avoid disputes, all of which are on record. Recently, when factories received warnings from the Public Concession Bureau and reported to the association, the association has always been running around and providing guidance to avoid losses from suspension of work and relocation. As a result, it was discovered that the Public Concession Bureau members' investigations of factories were entirely based on ideal assumptions and not based on facts at all. The errors are recorded below (two points see above). From these two points, it can be seen that the Public Concession Bureau did not seek specialized personnel for its investigations and did not take matters seriously. Even if the Westerners involved in the investigation, no matter how knowledgeable or experienced, could quickly understand the content, order, and working conditions of a certain industry in the shortest period of time, it is not only impossible in reason, but also not allowed by facts. Moreover, relying solely on the Westerner's own assumptions, the nitpicking investigations have been clearly demonstrated by the association's participation. However, the Public Concession Bureau used this as a basis to warn factories. Factories that are not proficient in English must hire someone to translate, and the translator's interpretation is then turned into Chinese, which is even further from the facts. How can they avoid wrongful suspension of work and wrongful relocation? This matter concerns the vital interests of factories, and one mistake cannot be allowed to be repeated. Therefore, a special letter is issued to all domestic goods factories: in the future, if you receive English letters from the Public Concession Bureau, you should return them immediately and ask them to translate them into Chinese before sending them back together with the original English letter, so that you can accept them and avoid errors. Please comply accordingly."

Measures to defend against humiliation. It is hoped that the people of the country will pay special attention to talents in aviation and aircraft manufacturing. It is reported that Chen and Pan plan to continue flying to Beiping after the engine of the Wang Que aircraft is modified, and then from Beiping to Guangxi to complete their flight plan.

Northeastern Refugee Relief Association Replied to Kong Xianrong Yesterday 117

Relief funds are exhausted and we cannot provide assistance

The Northeastern Refugee Relief Committee of this city received a letter from Kong Xianrong, deputy commander of Wang Delin's army, stating that the families of his troops in Shanghai were having difficulty making a living and requesting relief. However, we are honored with excessive praise, which we dare not accept. Now, your generals are either staying at the front or guarding new provinces, loyally defending the country, which we deeply admire. We are requested to continue to maintain support. This association is willing to make every effort to prevent the decline of our initial efforts. However, at present, relief funds are nearing exhaustion, and fundraising is becoming increasingly difficult. Moreover, this association is a temporary organization, and its duration is uncertain. The families of your generals staying in Shanghai should still be asked to devise a thorough and comprehensive plan for their future arrangements as soon as possible. We have stated our case frankly, and hope you will understand."

Coal and raw materials for steelmaking to be taken from Dangtu

Contract awaits Song's return to the country for signing

(5) Supervisor Pan Xulun proposed on an ad hoc basis that the donations received by the association now are relatively small, and the association's expenses should be saved. It was resolved to send a letter to the Standing Committee asking them to schedule a joint meeting of the Standing, Custodian, and Supervisory Committees to discuss whether the association should temporarily end or reduce its scope. (6) Supervisor Bei Zuyi proposed on an ad hoc basis that the association should announce to donors that they should pay attention to whether their names and the amount of their donations are recorded in the Creditworthiness Record. If their donation is not listed, please bring the receipt to the Supervisory Committee for inquiry in order to investigate. It was resolved to pass the proposal. (7) Supervisor Chen Peide proposed on an ad hoc basis that the previous joint meeting had proposed that all donations received by the association that were handed over to groups or individuals to be forwarded to the Northeastern Anti-Japanese generals should have their handwritten receipts submitted to the association for review and filing, which had already been resolved to be followed. However, it has not yet been implemented. Should the association send another letter to the Standing Committee to follow up? It was resolved to send a letter to the Standing Committee, asking them to handle the matter in accordance with the resolution within the scope possible. The meeting adjourned after the discussions.

Sino-Russian-German Air Transport Joint Operation Issue 120

Li Jingcong will return to Shanghai for detailed discussion

Central News Agency, Beijing: The trial flight between Dihua and Tacheng was successful, and the Sino-Russian-German joint air transport can be implemented on August 1. The reporter specially visited the Hangya Aviation Company to inquire. According to Secretary Zhenhu Tan, the head of the airline group, Walter, went to the stations in Xinjiang last week to discuss the matter, and the results were satisfactory. The radio station can be installed immediately, but it must wait until Manager Li returns before it can be decided. It will also take time to install the radio station, so the joint operation still needs to wait. The details of Mr. Cha's conversation are as follows:

Eurasian Joint Transport 121

Mr. Cha said that the main task of the company is to connect the direct transportation between Europe and Asia. Initially, there was a plan for direct air transport from Shanghai to Berlin, but due to the initial establishment of the company, the strength was insufficient, and the situation in Xinjiang was constantly changing, and various obstacles were unavoidable. Therefore, joint transport was carried out first. The German shareholder Lufthansa contacted the Russian side and obtained their consent. It was expected to be implemented in the spring of this year, but the matter was delayed due to sudden changes in Xinjiang. Now that the government has sent personnel to mediate, it is gradually becoming stable. Therefore, the head of the airline group of the company, the German Walter, took the plane west last Wednesday, stayed in Hami for an hour, and continued west. He stopped in Dihua for a day, and then went to Tacheng and other places in Xinjiang. The opinions on politics may not be completely consistent, but they all expressed their willingness to sincerely maintain the transportation business. Therefore, Mr. Hua's trip received a warm reception from the local authorities and achieved satisfactory results. Local telegrams had previously been prohibited from being set up by the provincial government, so navigation was very difficult. Now, the authorities have also approved the construction of the radio station after receiving the order.

Implementation Still Needs to Wait 122

Mr. Cha continued, "The radio stations in various places have not yet been built, and the situation in Xinjiang has not yet been fully stabilized. It is necessary to consider whether there will be any more incidents in the future. After the joint operation is implemented, mail between the two continents will be delivered on schedule through this fastest route. If an incident occurs in Xinjiang, transportation will be hindered, and the company's international reputation will inevitably be damaged. Therefore, there are no difficulties in terms of geography and weather for the implementation of this route. The reason for careful consideration is to avoid the impact of politics. Manager Li returned to Beijing last week to visit relatives, and is scheduled to come to Shanghai tomorrow on a China National Aviation Corporation flight from Beijing to Shanghai to discuss this matter in detail."

Lanzhou-Qinghai Branch Line 123

The Lanzhou-Qinghai branch line is not long and is easy to implement. However, there is no business in the area, only to connect the transportation in the interior. Since the line has no income, it requires local assistance. The Qinghai Provincial Government was previously informed and approved, but it was only a proposal. Li had a plan to fly to Qinghai recently to discuss the matter in person, but he was unable to do so due to illness. He will probably go after returning to Shanghai.

Ping-Shaanxi and Guangdong-Shaanxi 124

The company's plan for this year is to change the Ping-Luo line to pass through Taiyuan in Shanxi to Xi'an. The Guangdong-Hankou line will also be extended through Xiangyang to Xi'an, both of which will meet with the Northwest line. The two lines have been decided and will be completed this year. However, since the budget has not yet been determined and the approval of the Ministry of Communications is required, planning has not yet begun. However, it is hoped that it will be completed this year.

Soviet Russian Commercial Commissioner Gao Maofu Comes to China to Investigate Commerce 125

Plans to establish a Sino-Russian joint venture company in Tianjin

Capital set at eight million to fifteen million

Since the resumption of diplomatic relations between China and Russia, Russian goods have been selling well, while China's exports are the opposite. The biggest reason is that Russia's trade system is state-owned, while China's is still free trade. In order to control trade with Russia, the Ministry of Industry and Commerce has drafted a detailed plan to establish a trade bureau, which has been approved by the Central Political Council and handed over to the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for detailed consultation. At the same time, it is also planned to organize a Soviet Russian industrial inspection team with officials and merchants to learn from. However, the plan was delayed due to the Soviet Union's sale of the Middle East Railway. According to the International Trade Bureau, the Soviet Russian authorities have sent Commercial Commissioner Gao Maofu to China to develop the Russian goods market in China. He will go to Tianjin, Shanghai, Hong Kong, and other places to conduct on-the-spot investigations of China's commercial conditions. Xinxin News Agency reporters learned from another source that the task of Soviet Russian Commercial Commissioner Gao Maofu's visit to China, in addition to investigating the current state of commerce in China, is to establish a Sino-Russian commercial and civilian joint venture company in Tianjin with a capital of eight million to fifteen million, specializing in the export and import trade between China and Russia. It is also reported that the industrial authorities have paid attention to the joint venture company before the establishment of the bureau.

All Zhejiang Public Association Appeals for the People of Linhai County 131

Forced to subscribe to shares for the Xintian-Linhai Highway

The All Zhejiang Public Association submitted a document to the government, stating that Yao Yanwen, the magistrate of Linhai County, was illegally forcing people to subscribe to road shares, enriching himself and abusing the people, in order to raise funds for the construction of the Xintian-Linhai Highway. It is requested that he be dismissed from office and investigated, and that another method of raising funds be established to rebuild the road. The construction of highways in various counties is an implementation of developing transportation. If any people are able to do so within their financial means, they should contribute to help achieve it. The government offices in charge of road administration should also carefully plan the beginning, assess whether the construction of the road meets the local needs within the scope of the people's ability, and whether it is conducive to transportation and transportation, as well as the urgency, importance, difficulty, and ease of the project, with a comprehensive plan and accurate estimate. They should use peaceful and universal methods to persuade people to participate in the purchase of shares, and should not add any pressure, so that everyone will be suspicious, which will hinder the progress of road construction. However, this association has repeatedly received letters from Wang Shixian, Wang Shijin, Yang Dezhan, Zhang Yinshi, Wang Qichuan, Hu Heshang, Li Rongzhao, Ma Bingwen, Hu Shizhong, and others in Linhai, stating that Yao Yanwen, the magistrate of Linhai County, was raising funds for the construction of the Xintian-Linhai Highway. The method of raising funds was to divide the shares into two types, A and B. Type A was 10 yuan, and type B was 5 yuan. Those with more than five mu of real estate were assigned type B shares, and those with more than ten mu were assigned type A shares, and the rest were assigned in progressive amounts. The notice of collection of funds stated that if anyone refused to subscribe and pay, soldiers would be sent to arrest them and force them to pay, and they would also be charged for the expenses of the soldiers and officials. Not only were taxes levied according to the number of mu, but they were also robbed with military force, illegally arrested and detained, and additional supplies were greedily demanded. Their illegal abuse of the people was outrageous. As for Hu Heshang's letter, in addition to this method, those with only two or three mu of land were also required to pay 5 yuan or 10 yuan, without giving receipts. The civilian, who had no land, was assigned 15 yuan in shares, which was later reduced by 5 yuan. Because he refused, four members of the security regiment sent by the district arrested the civilian, tortured and looted him, and put him in shackles. Because his son went to the political and legal authorities to sue, his son A Zhao was also arrested and subjected to inhumane torture. His hands were tied behind his back and exposed to the scorching sun on a stone slab for an hour. Yang Dekan's letter stated that he was forced to subscribe to five shares of the Xintian-Linhai road shares by Wang Dingrui, the district chief of the district, with a deadline of three days. One day, he received a letter on the afternoon of the third day, and more than ten members of the security regiment came to force him to pay. They first demanded 4 yuan and 6 jiao for the expenses of the security personnel, and then dragged him to the security regiment, where he was shackled with wooden shackles and tied to a pillar. Later, he pawned three mu of land and exchanged the proceeds for a receipt of 25 yuan. Another 2 yuan was used for expenses before he was released. Their barbarity and cruelty were something that officials in the era of autocratic warlords dared not do, but they were seen under the party rule of Qingbai. How can we not be indignant? This case was approved by the Zhejiang Provincial Government on July 6 this year. The Linhai farmers, Yang Dezhan, and others, petitioned for relief from the forced subscription of funds for the Xintian-Linhai road. The approval stated that the case had been previously submitted by Li Rongzhao, Yu Wenguang, and Li Ding of the county, and the Ministry of Finance and Construction had been ordered to order the county magistrate to thoroughly investigate and report, and to quickly submit the method of raising funds for review. After the report was submitted to the government, it was ordered to wait for the county government to submit the report to the Ministry before reviewing it and reporting it. This approval shows that the method of raising funds has not yet been submitted for approval. The county magistrate is using the beautiful name of construction to carry out the abusive policies of extortion, disregarding the national law and ignoring the people's wishes. His boldness and recklessness are shocking. This association is saddened by the decline of official morality and the helplessness of the people. We do not hesitate to speak out and present this case on behalf of the people. We have attached a copy of the Linhai Fundraising Method for the Xintian-Linhai Highway and a genuine copy of the collection notice with the official seal. In addition to submitting separate petitions, we respectfully request the President to order the Executive Yuan to transfer the case to the Zhejiang Provincial Government, allowing (the Provincial Government to quickly) dismiss and investigate County Magistrate Yao Yanwen, as well as Wang Dingrui and others who assisted him in his abuse of power. At the same time, the method of raising funds that has not been approved should be revoked, and personnel should be sent to investigate the construction process of the highway and raise funds separately to rebuild the road, so as to improve road administration and relieve the people's difficulties. We cannot help but appeal and hope. Respectfully presented to National Government Chairman Lin, Executive Yuan President Wang, Zhejiang Provincial Government Chairman Lu, and Supervisory Yuan President Yu, by the chairman of the Shanghai All Zhejiang Public Association, Director Chu Fucheng.
