Jiangsu-Zhejiang Fish Industry Association Held Membership Representative Assembly Yesterday 133

Group meetings will continue today

The Shanghai Joint Office of the Jiangsu-Zhejiang Fish Industry Association held a plenary meeting of representatives at the association's headquarters on Sichuan Road at 2:00 pm yesterday to discuss the method of dealing with the fishery construction fee that cannot be collected by the fish market or contracted for the donation amount, and the important issue of organizing the Joint Association of Jiangsu-Zhejiang Sea Fish Industry Associations. Representatives from various places came to Shanghai to attend the meeting enthusiastically. The details of the meeting are recorded as follows:

Attending Representatives 134

Yuyao Huang Lianxiang, Cai Jinmu, Xu Gengfu, Wang Gongru, Taizhou Fang Youdu, Ningbo Xia Zubin, Hu Zhiting, Mao Anqing, Le Badong, Shaoxing Zhu Zhichuan, Shou Chang, Fang Wenyin, Chu Neniyu, Kunshan Zhu Fuzhen, Zhou Qingquan, Wuxing Sheng Menghua, Shipu Yang Shou Zeng, Xiaoshan Yuan Zhaozhen, Wen Jia Yan, Sun Fengyang, Zheng Meizhang, Shen Zhiqian, Shanghai Seafood Industry Shao Douxing, Zhou Chaogui, Ge Weian, Shanghai Salted Fish Industry Zhang Zhisheng, Chen Zuyu, Zheng Yunsheng, Shanghai Fresh Fish Industry Hu Diansun, Xu Yangshan, Liu Tonghua, Xu Shanxing, etc., a total of 67 people, Hu Diansun was publicly elected as chairman, and Xiang Yuqiao was the recorder.

Discussion of Various Cases 135

First, the Chairman reported on the situation of the Fisheries Construction Fee dispute and the process of mediation. Then, the discussion began. (1) Regarding the proposal to initiate the organization of the Joint Association of Zhejiang Seafood, Fresh and Salted Fish Industries, it is necessary to apply to the Party and government organs for a license. (Explanation) Since the eastward spread of European trends and the beginning of commercial warfare, the survival of the fittest has become a universal principle of natural selection. Chinese commerce has historically lacked organization and research, let alone our industry. Once it suffers even a slight foreign insult, it is caught completely unprepared. If we do not strengthen our organization and thoroughly explore matters, how can we stand firm in the world? It was decided that (A) applications should be submitted to the Party and government organs for the issuance of licenses; before obtaining a license, an initiators' meeting should be organized first; (B) representatives of local industry associations can attend as initiators; (C) Fang Wenying, Hu Diansun, Mao Anqing, Ge Weian, Fang Youdu, Zhang Zhisheng, Le Qidong, and seven others were elected as representatives responsible internally and externally; (D) Hu Diansun was mutually elected as the chief representative. (2) Regarding the eight opinions previously proposed, a request was made to reconsider the case. It was decided to amend and pass them. (The original text has been published in previous reports, so it is omitted here.) (3) Regarding the Fisheries Construction Fee, which has not yet been resolved, what should be done? (Explanation) Although this case has been mediated three times by three mediators, the focus remains on treating fishing and fish as one. Fishing is fishing, and the Ministry of Industry has explained this. Moreover, the Fisheries Law stipulates in its very first article that fishing includes both harvesting and aquaculture. Therefore, this construction fee should clearly be collected from those engaged in harvesting and aquaculture. Our industry deals in fresh, dried, and salted seafood, which is nothing more than fishmongering and buying and selling between merchants. It is by no means fishing by fishermen. It is a direct transaction between the fishing merchant and the industry. How can we collect on their behalf? We have earnestly stated our case to the authorities, but they have not understood. It was decided that (A) if the government authorities exert too much pressure, then during the critical period, all localities should uniformly adopt emergency and effective response measures (secret); (B) when necessary, representatives should be sent to Beijing to petition. It was decided that the petition representatives would be the previously elected responsible representatives; (C) regarding the measures in item A, each representative should discuss them further with their respective associations and submit their written opinions by August 10th for comprehensive review and handling. (4) It was decided that a small group meeting would be held at 4:00 PM on the 30th (today). The meeting adjourned at 6:00 PM after the discussions.

Meng Lujiu Resigns 136

Representative Meng Lujiu, who previously joined this office and consistently held its positions, suddenly telegraphed the office a few days ago, stating that, regarding the case of collecting the Fisheries Construction Fee, after three mediations by Mr. Yu Qiaqing, Du Yuesheng, and Yu Zuoting, our association has declared its withdrawal. Hereafter, our association will not be involved in any of your office's affairs. This is telegraphed for your information. Respectfully, the entire membership of the Hangzhou City Ham, Cured Meat, and Dried Fish Industry Association.

All Workers of the Shanghai Power Company Petitioned the City Party Headquarters Yesterday 137

Over 1,600 Workers Braved the Heat and Walked to Request Resumption of Work and Improved Treatment

According to the Guomin News Agency, the Shanghai Power Company dismissed Ni Wenfu, Pan Genlin, Chen Baogen, and Zhang Caisheng, directors and staff respectively, of the Fourth District (Shanghai) Water and Electricity Industry Workers' Union. It also refused to accept improved treatment conditions, causing resentment among all workers, which led to a labor strike. For a month now, despite repeated mediation by Party and government organs and Chinese directors such as Yuan Ludeng of the Municipal Council, no resolution has been reached. Over 1,600 workers from the company sent representatives to the City Party Headquarters yesterday afternoon, holding a petition requesting assistance in resuming work and improving treatment conditions. They also distributed a declaration. Details are recorded below.

Workers Departed. Over 1,600 workers from the company's new factory in Yangshupu, Hongkou, and the old factory on Fielun Road, due to the Public Concession authorities preventing gatherings, departed from the two locations in succession yesterday afternoon at 2:00 PM and walked to Xinbeimen, where they gathered, organized, and divided into five teams: Negotiation, Rescue, Discipline, Transportation, and General Command. They were led by a white cloth banner reading "Petitioning Group of Shanghai Power Company Workers." Each worker wore a white cloth armband. They walked along Minguo Road to the City Party Headquarters to petition. The District Head of the Second District received the information and dispatched patrol officer Long Daozhen, police chief Rao Zengcheng, and 24 police officers, along with detectives Wang Shaohua and Wang Yushan from the Garrison Headquarters Investigation Team, to maintain order.

Request for Assistance. The workers stood respectfully in front of the City Party Headquarters, sweating profusely under the scorching sun. They elected Dai Rensi, Lou Yongquan, Jiang Zhongming, Bao Defu, and Chen Miaosheng as representatives. Led by Ni Wenfu, the executive director of the union, they entered the headquarters. Dai Youheng, a staff member of the Civil Affairs Section of the City Party Headquarters, received them. The representatives first reported the circumstances of the labor strike and requested assistance in restoring work and improving treatment conditions. They raised four points regarding the company: (1) Reinstate Ni Wenfu and the other three; (2) The company must pay workers a 5% pension and an additional month's salary as a year-end bonus each year; (3) Those who die on duty should receive a subsidy of 2,000 yuan as compensation; (4) The company shall not dismiss workers without cause in the future; if the company is unable to maintain employment and lays off workers, it must pay three months' severance pay, etc. They also submitted a petition and a declaration. Dai gave some encouragement and expressed his willingness to provide as much assistance as possible and engage in appropriate negotiations with the company. The representatives were satisfied. They dispersed around 4:00 PM.

International Telecommunications Bureau Stops Accepting Collect Telegrams to the US and Canada 138

Effective August 1st

The International Telecommunications Bureau of the Ministry of Communications, due to significant fluctuations in international exchange rates, has been collecting telegram fees from recipients for all telegrams sent to the United States. After calculation, this often results in losses compared to Chinese prices. In order to maintain operations, it announced yesterday that, effective August 1st, all collect telegrams (including government and news telegrams) sent via radio or submarine cable to (1) the United States, (2) Canada, (3) Newfoundland, (4) Saint Pierre and Miquelon, and (5) Hawaii will no longer be accepted.

Pirates Attack and Assault Yangtze River Steamer near Matouzhen 139

Jiang'an Steamer Hit by Bullets, Passengers Injured

Shipping Industry Asks for Warships to Suppress Pirates

In recent years, bandits in the upper reaches of the Yangtze River have gradually become less visible, and steamers have sailed more safely. However, above Hankou, escorts are still needed to protect the waterways. Unexpectedly, recently, a large number of bandits emerged near Wuxue, across the river, to attack steamers in an attempt to plunder them. This time, the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Jiang'an steamer was attacked, resulting in injuries to passengers and bullet damage to the ship's hull. The details are being investigated and reported as follows:

Jiang'an Sailing Downstream to Shanghai 140

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Yangtze River steamer Jiang'an is one of the largest in the company's fleet of Yangtze River steamers. This time, on the 26th of this month, it sailed downstream from Hankou, carrying a large number of goods and passengers, heading back to Shanghai. Due to the high water level of the river, it followed the order of the Jianghai Customs and switched to slow speed, as fast speed might erode the riverbank and cause damage. On the morning of the 27th, the ship sailed below Huangzhou, approaching Wuxue, when it suddenly encountered a large number of bandits attempting to plunder the ship. The bandits opened fire on the Jiang'an steamer, endangering passengers.

Upper Reaches Bandits Plan to Plunder 141

When the Jiang'an steamer arrived at Wuxue, it was 6:25 AM on the 27th. At this time, it was sailing downstream at slow speed, with the ship sailing in the center of the river. Suddenly, the sound of gunfire was heard from across the river from Wuxue. This area had been peaceful for a long time. Upon hearing this alarm, the crew quickly observed the opposite bank of Wuxue and saw a large number of bandits, about three hundred and several dozen, seemingly coming from Matouzhen. They separated on the riverbank and opened fire on the Jiang'an steamer, intending to force the Jiang'an to stop. The passengers on the ship panicked as the bandits tried to board and plunder the ship. The captain immediately ordered the ship to sail closer to the Wuxue side to avoid the bullets and sped up towards Jiujiang.

Passenger Injury Situation 142

These bandits were well-equipped with firearms, but their clothing and attire were entirely like poor farmers, some wearing blue cloth shirts and trousers, some barefoot. The bandit group also had a red flag. Fortunately, there were no small boats on the river, so the bandits could only chase the Jiang'an steamer along the riverbank. It was found that this place is in Ruichang County, Jiangxi Province, and the opposite bank belongs to Hubei Province. At the time, the Jiang'an steamer was fortunate to evade the attack, so it did not suffer serious damage. However, when the bandits fired bullets indiscriminately, one third-class passenger was shot in the head. Fortunately, the bullet only grazed his head, and his life was not in danger. The other passengers were ordered by the captain to lie on the ship's deck, so although the windows of the dining room were hit by stray bullets, the passengers were not harmed. The injured passenger has arrived in Shanghai and is receiving medical treatment on his own.

Captain Reports to Shanghai 143

After being hit by bullets, the Jiang'an steamer sailed closer to the Wuxue bank, out of reach of the bandits' bullets, and arrived safely in Jiujiang. According to Jiang'an, when it departed from Hankou this time, there were several important military officers traveling in the dining room. After encountering the bandits, they promised to report to Chairman Chiang Kai-shek in Ganzhou and dispatch troops to suppress the bandits as soon as possible to ensure the safety of the waterways. Yesterday, the Jiang'an steamer arrived in Shanghai, and the captain reported to the head office about the bandit encounter near Matouzhen and the injury to passengers. He also requested that someone be sent to inspect the bullet damage on the ship and repair it immediately. At the same time, he requested that the head office telegraph the Navy Department to quickly send warships to the upper reaches of the Yangtze River to suppress the bandits near Matouzhen across from Wuxue, in order to ensure the safety of passengers and ships.

Smuggling Case at the Customs House Has Been Sent to the Local Court for Investigation 148

Seven More Accomplices Recently Arrested

Many Individuals Have Accumulated Great Wealth Through Smuggling

Many Customs Brokers Are Involved in the Conspiracy

The large-scale smuggling case involving clerks and others at the Jianghai Customs House has been reported in previous newspapers. It is now known that the case is currently being investigated by the Western Detective Chief Pontius, Deputy Detective McKeough, and Chinese Detectives Cheng Yongnian, Sun Fubi, Wang Haiquan, Shen Changshan, Wang Songsheng, Hu Changqing, Gu Wenkui, and others, working together. The investigation has been completed, and the entire case has been sent to the Local Court for investigation. The course of events is recorded as follows:

Significant Loss of National Revenue 149

For the past three years, a portion of all import taxes reported to the Jianghai Customs House has been subject to tax evasion and smuggling, resulting in incalculable losses to customs revenue. However, no concrete evidence could be found for prosecution. Therefore, the Customs Anti-Smuggling Section of the Customs Department ordered the Customs Water Police to investigate.

Distribution of Smuggling Proceeds 150

After receiving the order, the Water Police Chief assigned the above detectives to investigate separately. On the 20th of this month, reliable information was obtained stating that a fictitious office was set up inside the United Company at Room 208, 3rd Floor, No. 3 Hankou Road, with a small secret room. It had no legitimate business and was connected to Customs clerks who would stamp forged seals on the green and white customs declarations for large import taxes and secretly take them to the United Company. The forged declarations were stamped with forged seals by Customs clerks to pass them through at a lower price. At the same time, they solicited orders from foreign companies, and customs brokers colluded to commit fraud. It was also found that the manager was Shao Pengfei and the assistant manager was Su Kunnian. The smuggling proceeds were divided into ten shares, with the clerks receiving 35%, the customs brokers 40%, and the company 25%.

All Necessary Documents Available 151

After the investigation was clear, because the location was in the Public Concession, a request was made to the court to issue a search warrant. The Central Police Station on Sima Road dispatched Chinese and Western detectives to the United Company and searched. A small leather suitcase was found, containing 61 forged seals and genuine and forged green and white declarations (about three or four months' worth, previous ones had been destroyed). It was also found that the genuine declaration for nine automobiles reported on the 18th of this month by De Feng Foreign Company on Beijing Road had been removed and replaced with a forged one. The above seals covered all procedures for declaring imported goods, paying taxes, and issuing bills of lading from within the Customs House. Su Kunnian and six others present were arrested.

Seven More Individuals Subsequently Arrested 152

On the same day, it was also discovered that Han Jincai, formerly a clerk residing at No. 28, Lane 810, Xihua Road, had retired because he had accumulated a great deal of profit. He took a concubine and lived a leisurely life. Detectives rushed to the scene. Han was still bathing and having his back scrubbed by his concubine when he was taken away. This greatly spoiled the scene. As a result of this investigation, six more clerks were arrested: Shi Cunjiao, Wu Yueren, Wei Anxiang, Zhang Qiutao, Chen Zhongshan, and Shen Guozhang. It is rumored that there are many others involved in the smuggling at the Customs House, and many have fled after hearing the news.

Investigation of Customs Brokers 153

It was also discovered that customs brokers from the following foreign companies colluded to commit fraud: Ruifeng Foreign Company on Beijing Road, Meizuishi Foreign Company at No. 19 Jiujiang Road, Kaili Foreign Company at No. 17 Bowuyuan Road, Deji Foreign Company at No. 12 Bund, Yuxingxiang Company at No. 74 Renzhili, North Sichuan Road, Huajia Foreign Company at No. 2 Guangdong Road, Xincheng Foreign Company at No. 7 Yideli, Zililai Street, China Soap Company at No. 18 Huangpu Road, etc. Chen Guoliang, a customs broker from the China Soap Company, has been arrested, but the others have fled. They are currently being pursued.

Statistics on Smuggling Incidents 154

After Su Kunnian was arrested, he stated that the United Company was the Huayang Company three months ago, and Wang Yushu was the manager. They had been doing this for about two years, about four or five times a month, for a total of over 100 times. Each time, about ten or more people could divide 500 or 600 yuan from the 35% share. The procedures were so sophisticated that even senior officials could not detect them. The people involved in the past are all wealthy now. The clerks Wang Yueren, Shi Cunjiao, Wei Anxiang, etc., admitted that they each received 600 yuan for the Ruifeng Foreign Company's nine automobile case. Therefore, Shu Bo from the Anti-Smuggling Section of the Tax Office also went to court yesterday to apply for prosecution. The prosecutor ordered the defendant to be detained. Judge Xiao Xiefen briefly questioned Lin and ordered Lin Ziruan to provide bail so that he could be summoned at any time. After the investigation is clear, the hearing will be rescheduled for August 1st.

Local Ruffians Are Extremely Ferocious 155

Huang A'mei's Extortion Attempt Fails

He Steals and Uses an Axe to Attack People

Shen Youzhang, the owner of the Huazhang Construction Factory on Hongqiao Road, is located at No. 276 Yangjialou Road, owned by the Public Works Department. He recently contracted a construction project next to the factory. When construction began in June of this year, Huang A'mei, a local ruffian, went to the factory on the 25th of the same month to demand customary fees. The factory owner, Shen Youzhang, was not at the factory at the time. The ruffian left a business card and said he would come back in three days. If they did not pay, he would "give them a piece of his mind." Unexpectedly, that night, nineteen pieces of pine lumber and one water tap, worth about one hundred yuan, were lost. The factory owner reported it to the Sixth District First Police Station, and Huang A'mei was arrested and sent to the Public Security Bureau for transfer to the court for trial. However, at about 1:00 AM the night before last, a group of thirty or forty thugs, traveling in cars, armed with pistols, axes, and daggers, surrounded the factory, opened the factory gate, and declared that they were avenging Huang A'mei. At that time, only two watchmen, Mao Niande and Shen Changxing, were on night duty. The thugs, without asking any questions, brutally beat the two watchmen. Mao Niande's legs were slashed three times with an axe, and Shen Changxing was stabbed in the back and legs with a dagger. Both fell to the ground in extreme pain, bleeding profusely. Seeing that their goal had been achieved, the thugs looted three bags of water pipe elbows, worth about 400 yuan, before leaving in their cars. Afterwards, the factory owner, Shen Youzhang, arrived after hearing the alarm and sent the two injured watchmen to the Haig Road Red Cross Hospital for treatment. He also reported the incident to the Sixth District Headquarters and the Sixth District First Police Station, urging them to severely arrest the thugs and bring them to justice. It is said that the factory owner, Shen Youzhang, believes that this group of ruffians and gangsters has many accomplices and dared to take revenge and commit robbery with weapons at night. If they are not severely punished, how can public order be maintained and the law upheld? Yesterday, he again submitted a report to the Municipal Public Security Bureau, requesting that the court be asked to return the ruffian Huang A'mei for questioning his accomplices in order to detain and prosecute them according to the law.

Method for Sending Airmail 156

Indicate Route Clearly for Sorting

According to Shanghai Post Office news, airmail and parcels can be sent by the sender specifying a certain segment of the route to be sent by air, while the rest of the route is sent by ordinary mail. However, this is limited to cases where it can actually reduce the delivery time and the required postage is fully paid. All airmail and parcels sent in this way should clearly indicate the route specified for air transport on the envelope or parcel cover to facilitate sorting and avoid errors. It is even more appropriate to indicate this next to the (Airmail) printed on the prescribed airmail envelope or blue label.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Notifies All Industries to Prohibit Cash Prizes 157

Yesterday, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to various industry associations, ordering them to prohibit commercial companies from offering cash prizes. The original letter stated: "Respected Sirs, on the 27th of this month, we received Instruction No. 13855 from the Social Affairs Bureau, which stated: 'Regarding compliance matters, we have received Municipal Government Instruction No. 6295, which forwarded Finance Ministry Letter No. 6725, stating that the central government's issuance of Aviation and Highway Construction Lottery Tickets is related to major construction plans and is currently being actively promoted. Therefore, it is not permissible for other organs, groups, companies, or stores to imitate this. The China East Tobacco Company's awarding of lottery tickets is tantamount to printing counterfeit tickets, as is the Swiss-Luen Tobacco Company's Company Brand Champagne Coupons, the Fuxin Company's Holmes Brand Promotion Coupons, the Huapin Tobacco Company's Golden Arrow Brand Sales Promotion Coupons, and the Great Southeast Tobacco Company's High and Rich Coupons. Although the names are different, they all involve cash prizes. If it is for commercial competition, other methods of attracting customers should be devised, always adhering to the principle of not using cash rewards for customers so as not to hinder the government's major construction plans. From now on, if other tobacco companies and commercial companies still offer similar cash prizes, please pay special attention and stop them at any time.' We have recorded this order and forwarded it to you. We hereby instruct your association to notify its members that if they are offering cash prizes, they should stop immediately and devise other methods of attracting customers in order to comply with government orders."

International Drug Trafficking Case: Yan Ziliang Found Guilty 161

丨Sentenced to Three Years in Prison丨

The case of Yan Ziliang in the international drug trafficking organization has been concluded. The sentencing was held yesterday morning at 10:30 a.m. in the First Criminal Court, presided over by Judge Wang. The police attorney, Yuan Jiahan, appeared in court, and lawyer Wu Youyuan represented the defendant Yan Ziliang, who was said to be feeling unwell due to the summer heat and unable to attend court. The judge then stood up and read out the main text of the judgment: Yan Ziliang is sentenced to two years of imprisonment for manufacturing opium substitutes, and fined 4,000 yuan. If the fine is commuted to imprisonment, it will be calculated based on the ratio of the total fine to the number of days in a year. The number of days of detention before the final judgment will be deducted at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. One package of "Red Pills" (weighing five catties and twelve taels), two small packages of "White Nine" (weighing twelve taels), one package of "Black Pills" (weighing three taels), four sets of pill-making machines, five glass containers (containing medicinal powder), half a jar of opium (weighing one catty), one package of medicinal powder (eleven catties), one magnetic mortar, and one pestle will be confiscated and burned. The two confiscated account books will also be confiscated. The defendant remains on bail pending appeal.

A Bomb Was Thrown at Chen Fengh Heng Cotton Cloth Shop Last Night 164

The Chen Fengh Heng Cotton Cloth Shop at 190 Avenue Edward VII is a cotton cloth shop founded by Wang Qingchen (60 years old), a merchant from Yangzhou. It is one of the major cotton cloth shops in the area of Rue du Consulat, employing more than 20 clerks. It has been open for more than eight years and its business has been quite successful. Last night, at around 7:00 p.m., while the clerks were having dinner in the back hall, someone threw a bomb into the shop from the street. With a loud bang, the explosion shook the neighborhood, and passersby scattered. The police station of the Great Clock Tower was nearby, and the head constable, 各米也立, immediately led Western detective 巨也脫, Chinese detective Wu Wengang, and others to the scene to investigate. Only eight glass windows were damaged, and no one was injured. Detective Wu found several pieces of the damaged bomb casing on the ground and took them back to the police station for investigation.

Old Clerk Falls from Ladder While Repairing Large Flag and Dies Tragically 165

The Horizontal Support of the Ladder Suddenly Breaks

Seriously Injured by the Fall and Cannot Be Saved

Yu Weiqing, a native of Ningbo, 42 years old, worked as an old clerk in the Shi Weiji Clock Shop at 474 Nanking Road. At around 11:00 a.m. the day before yesterday, the shop's large signboard flag was suddenly blown by the wind, causing it to lean. The shop ordered Weiqing to repair it on the third floor. Unexpectedly, when he reached the top of the ladder, one of the horizontal supports he was standing on suddenly broke, causing him to fall. He was seriously injured. A colleague, Zhou Zhongyong, saw what happened and immediately told the shop owner, who sent him to the Renji Hospital for treatment, but it was ineffective, and he died soon after. The hospital reported to the Old Gate Police Station, which ordered Detective Pang Yutang to investigate. The body was taken to the Fei Lun Road Mortuary. Yesterday morning, Judge Guo Wei from the First Special District Local Court was dispatched to the mortuary to examine the body. Zhou Zhongyong testified that Yu also worked in the shop and was on duty that day when he saw that the flag outside was crooked, so the shop ordered Yu and the deceased to repair it. He had placed the bamboo ladder outside the window on the third floor, and the deceased had run up to repair it, while he was at the bottom of the ladder to prevent it from falling. Unexpectedly, when he reached the highest point, the support he was standing on suddenly broke, causing him to fall. Judge Guo accepted the testimony and ruled that the deceased Yu Weiqing died from a head injury caused by the fall. The body was handed over to his wife, Yu Wangshi, to be taken back for burial.

Director of the Shanghai Office of the Pseudo-Capital Bank Fined for Smoking Opium 166

The Yitong Bank of the pseudo-capital Changchun recently established an office in Shanghai, located on the third floor of the Yongheng Bank at 266 Ningbo Road. Li Linshu, a native of Hubei, was appointed as the director of the office. Li had a smoking habit, and spent all day lying in bed. Suspect in Murder Case from a Year Ago Arrested Today 167

Xu Rongxing, a native of Ningbo with the nickname "Chai Pian A Mao," living at 49 Songcun, Rue Kraetzer in the French Concession, was gambling mahjong at the Zonghui Club opened by Ding Yaokui in the east wing of the building at 2 Yuqing Lane, West Xinqiao Street, at 11:15 p.m. on January 19 of last year, when he was suddenly shot and killed by his enemy Li Shurong, also known as "White-Eyed Shurong," and his gang. Dachang Public Security Bureau Solves the Case of the Murder of the Township Head 168

Two Suspects in the Case of the Couple and Their Unborn Child

Confiscated Two Submachine Guns and Three Rifles

Yesterday morning at around 10:00 a.m., the Dachang Township Public Security Bureau in Baoshan County received a report from Yang Zhibiao, the head of the seventh jia of the second district of the Dachang Township Security Corps, stating that Hua Apei, who lived in Dachang Township and ran a noodle shop, had a submachine gun and sold it to Zhu Qiuting, the vice-head of his jia. This gun was the same gun that was used to kill Chen Mingxian, the township head of Chenjiabaixiang Township and the head of the Security Corps, and his wife and unborn child. He requested that Hua Apei be summoned for questioning. After hearing the report, the director of the Bureau, Liu Guiting, immediately sent police to summon Hua. According to Hua Apei's confession, he was working on the west side of the Xiyue Temple Road on the 28th or 29th of last month when he saw a gun exposed next to his deceased brother's coffin, took it back and hid it, and entrusted a villager, Xu Anbang, to sell it to Zhu Qiuting, the vice-head of the seventh jia of the second district of the Security Corps, for 45 yuan, of which 30 yuan had been paid. He admitted that he had handed over the gun to Zhu Qiuting to take away. After obtaining the confession, the questioning officer sent police, led by villager Xu Anbang and Chen Jinxian, the brother of the deceased township head Chen Mingxian, to search next to Hua Apei's deceased brother's coffin. Unexpectedly, they found two submachine guns and two rifles. One Russian-style rifle had a Baoshan County brand mark, confirming that it was the gun of the deceased Chen Mingxian. They were all brought back to the Bureau. Also, at around 3:00 p.m. the day before yesterday, the Bureau received a report from the plaintiff Chen Jinxian stating that a man named Wu Hai was peddling a gun bolt in Chenjiabaixiang. Later, he sold two more to Jin Yuanyi for 21 yuan each. When Wu brought the two gun bolts, they detained him and reported to the Bureau. Upon interrogation, Wu Hai confessed that he was 26 years old, a native of Tongzhou, and lived in Yanjiata. The gun bolt was entrusted to him by a man named Xiao Xu to sell, so he went to Chenjiabaixiang to sell it to Jin Yuanyi for 21 yuan. He admitted that it was true, but he only took 10 yuan at that time. Later, Jin asked him if he had any more gun bolts, so he sent two more today (i.e., the day before yesterday), but they were caught. Later, Director Liu asked him if he knew anything about the shooting of Chen Mingxian. He replied that he did not know, but he did sell guns. On November 24 of last year, he, Chen Hongtao, and Zhou Zhaoyue bought 610 bullets from Chen Ming, and were caught by the Shanghai Public Security Bureau's Detective Team while passing through Zhenru and served a three-month sentence. After verifying the confession, the questioning officer sent police to the Zhabei Fourth District Public Security Bureau and police detectives to arrest Xiao Xu at the Tanziqiao this morning (i.e., yesterday morning) and bring him back to the Bureau. Upon interrogation, Xiao Xu confessed that his surname was Yu, his name was Dasan, he was 32 years old, and he was a native of Funing. He did not admit that his surname was Xu. He lowered his head and stammered about the matter of entrusting him to sell the gun bolt. Director Liu suspected that the defendants were involved in the case of the shooting of Chen Mingxian and his wife, as well as his pregnant child, in Chenjiabaixiang, and the theft of the guns, so he ordered that the defendants Wu Hai and Xiao Xu (i.e., Yu Dasan), together with the three gun bolts and the three rifles and two submachine guns in the Hua Apei case, be sent to the Baoshan County Government for trial at around 4:00 p.m. yesterday.

Zhang Er, a Suspect in the Baoshan Kidnapping Case, Arrested 169

Zhang Er, a native of Qingkou, 34 years old, fled to Shanghai after committing the crime of colluding with others to kidnap people and extort ransoms in Baoshan County. He lived at 29 Fulan Lane, 157 Pingliang Road. The day before yesterday, Wang Shouzhang, the captain of the Fifth District Detective Team of the Baoshan County Public Security Bureau, came to Shanghai based on the confession of the arrested Li Changqing, and reported to the Yulin Road Police Station. The detectives went to the address and arrested Zhang Er. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Local Court. Judge Xiao Xiefen interrogated him. Police attorney Zhang Tianyin stated that according to the investigation by Wang Shouzhang, the captain of the Detective Team of the Baoshan Public Security Bureau, the defendant, together with the arrested Li Changqing, kidnapped nine members of Li Fengming's family on August 22 of last year and extorted a large sum of money before fleeing to Shanghai. Now, Baoshan County Magistrate Jin has sent an official letter requesting that the defendant be transferred. If Zhang admits to being involved, he does not object to the transfer; otherwise, please detain him and wait for Li Changqing to be brought to court for questioning next time to comply with the agreed procedures. He then presented the county's official letter. Detective Team Captain Wang Shouzhang claimed that all nine members of the Li family had been released long ago. According to Li Changqing's confession, the defendant participated in the discussion before the kidnapping and was responsible for guarding the hostages after the kidnapping. He had planned to bring Li Changqing to court to identify the defendant, but he was afraid that it would be inconvenient and unexpected events would occur en route. Moreover, the victim is a villager, and according to local customs, they are timid and unwilling to come to court to testify. He then presented Li Changqing's confession. Zhang Er, when questioned, firmly denied any involvement in the kidnapping case and said that he did not know Li Changqing either. He should be investigated. The police attorney also stated that the case should be postponed and Li should be brought to the court to testify. More detectives should be prepared to protect him during the journey. Judge Xiao reviewed the confession and ordered the defendant to be returned to custody, ordering the Baoshan Public Security Bureau to provide relevant evidence for review.

Apprentice Drowns at Zhengxing Restaurant 170

Zhou Abing, an 18-year-old Ningbo native who was an apprentice at the Hua Zhengxing Restaurant on Huaji Road in Hongkou, jumped into the river at the Shuntai Wharf in Hongkou yesterday afternoon at 1:00 p.m. to swim. Because he was not familiar with the water, he could not support himself when the big waves came, and he sank to the bottom of the river and drowned tragically. The fellow swimmer immediately reported to the restaurant, and the restaurant sent people to the attack site to salvage the body, but it was not found. They then sent a waiter, Zhang Abing, to report to the Customs Water Patrol Police Station, ordering the police to pay attention to the body at any time.

Woman Dies from Ingesting Raw Opium 171

Pan Zhangshi, 44 years old, from Jiangsu, lived at 21 Zui Lai Street in the French Concession. Yesterday afternoon at 4:30 p.m., for some unknown reason, she suddenly had the idea of ending her life and secretly ingested raw opium to commit suicide. Her family noticed and rushed her to Renji Hospital, but because she had taken too much poison, the treatment was ineffective, and she died at around 5:00 p.m. The body was transferred to the morgue for examination.

Arts and Entertainment 175

Far East Hotel Yue Opera: The Far East Hotel on Xizang Road, in view of the variety of entertainment options in Shanghai, but lacking high-class Yue Opera, specially dispatched commissioners to Yue County last month to invite famous Yue Opera performers to Shanghai. They will perform Yue Opera (i.e., Shaoxing Opera) in the hotel's southern theater. Every night, they will stage lengthy, cautionary dramas. Since the opening performance a month ago, they have been very well received by society. Every show is sold out. Before 8 pm, the "Full House" sign is hung high at the door. The plays are mostly long, often lasting more than ten hours, and some can even run for two or three days and nights. The plots are tight, and each scene is uniquely wonderful, which is why they are praised by the people of Shanghai. In addition, the hotel is located near the racecourse, with naturally good air circulation, so fans are not needed, and the natural breeze is another advantage that other places cannot match, and viewers gather there. As for the famous Yue Opera performers, almost all of them have been recruited, such as veteran actor Xiao Fengcai, Wu Changshun, flower actress Xiao Yueying, young actor Wang Guifa, two-faced Gai Yumi, Lu Changsheng, etc., who are all leaders of Yue Opera. Those who understand Yue Opera praise them highly. It is said that they will soon perform seasonal plays.

Moreover, the location is convenient, the seats are comfortable, the air conditioning is all around, and the atmosphere is elegant and pleasant. Being there, one forgets the summer heat. The people of Shanghai can broaden their horizons. It is scheduled to open tomorrow night. Lao Yu Li Xiang Troupe Scheduled to perform Cinematic Opera: The Chaozhou Lao Yu Li Xiang Troupe, after participating in the Chaozhou Fellow Association's entertainment performance, was retained by the Chaozhou fellows and continued to perform at the Empire Theater. The Yangtze River Basin and the coastal areas north of Taiwan are hot and cloudy, with a slight chance of local showers. The wind is from the southeast. Its center at about 6:00 am was within 60 miles of the intersection of 20 degrees north latitude and 120 degrees east longitude. The wind is strong. The center of another hurricane in the Pacific Ocean at about 2:00 pm was within 120 miles of the intersection of 14 degrees north latitude and 133 degrees east longitude, moving northwest. Educational News Highlights

School Militarization 181

Adding Buglers to High Schools and Above

(Nanjing, 29th) The Ministry of Education issued an order on the 29th that high schools and above may add one bugler to play bugle calls and be responsible for all duties related to military training.

Private College Students Allowed to Take Entrance Exams 182

(Nanjing, 29th) The Ministry of Education issued a notice on the 29th to all universities that graduates and students of private vocational schools and above that have not been registered or have been closed, after screening and passing the examinations and students who have been demoted, holding the transfer certificates for the final grade issued by the Ministry, should be allowed to take the entrance exams when the schools enroll students, in order to provide relief.

Cultural Academy Students Petition the Ministry 183

(Central News Agency, Nanjing, 29th) Seven student representatives from the Cultural Academy Nursing School, including Wang Shiying, went to the Ministry of Education on the 29th to ask for the revocation of the order to stop the school and to allow a one-year trial period. The secretary, Zhou Tu, met with them on behalf of the minister and replied that the national education policy focuses on agriculture, industry, medicine, and science, and supports schools with excellent performance in cultural subjects and cancels those that are not good, without leniency. He also promised to convey the students' petition to the minister and asked the representatives to return to the ministry on the morning of the 31st to receive the minister's response.

National Tsinghua University Examines Subjects for Studying in the United States 184

National Tsinghua University, in accordance with the will of the Ministry of Education this year, will examine students for publicly funded study in the United States. The subjects for the exam have been determined by the expert committee and are divided into two types: general and specialized. The general subjects are Party Ideology, Chinese, English, and a second foreign language (German or French). The specialized exam subjects are as follows:

(1) Applied Optics and Instrument Manufacturing, with additional exams in Optics, Mechanics, Electromagnetism (including Applied Electricity), Calculus and Differential Equations, and General Knowledge of Technology; (2) Vacuum Tube Manufacturing, with additional exams in Mechanics, Electromagnetism, Calculus and Differential Equations, Vacuum Tubes and Their Applications, and General Knowledge of Technology; (3) Applied Geophysics, with additional exams in Mechanics, Elasticity Theory, Electricity, Magnetism, Calculus and Differential Equations, and General Geology; (4) Steel Metallurgy, with additional exams in Optics, Calculus, General Electrical Engineering, Applied Mechanics and Material Mechanics, and Theoretical Chemistry (including Thermodynamics); (5) Steelmaking, with additional exams in Calculus, Thermal Engineering, General Electrical Engineering, Inorganic Chemistry (including Inorganic Analysis), and Applied Mechanics and Material Mechanics; (6)

Ordnance Ballistics, with additional exams in Mechanics, Advanced Mechanics, Theoretical Chemistry (including Thermodynamics), Calculus and Differential Equations, and Electromagnetism; (7)

Ordnance Gun Manufacturing, with additional exams in Thermal Engineering, Mechanical Design, General Electrical Engineering, Calculus and Differential Equations, and Applied Mechanics and Material Mechanics; (8) National Defense Chemistry and Sulfuric Acid Manufacturing, with additional exams in Inorganic Chemistry, Organic Chemistry, Theoretical Chemistry, Industrial Chemistry, General Physics, and General Mechanical Engineering; (9) Aircraft Engine, with additional exams in Calculus, Internal Combustion Engine, Mechanical Design, General Electrical Engineering, and Applied Mechanics and Material Mechanics; (10) Aircraft Airframe, with additional exams in Structural Mechanics, Thermal Engineering, General Electrical Engineering, Calculus and Differential Equations, and Applied Mechanics and Material Mechanics; (11) Water Conservancy River Engineering, with additional exams in Hydraulics, Structural Mechanics, Calculus, Water Conservancy Engineering, and Applied Mechanics and Material Mechanics; (12) Water Conservancy Hydropower, with additional exams in Hydraulics, Structural Mechanics, Calculus, General Electrical Engineering, and Applied Mechanics and Material Mechanics; (13) Crop Breeding, with additional exams in Crop Science, Breeding, Genetics, Biostatistics, and Plant Physiology; (14) Soil Fertilizer, with additional exams in Crop Science, Fertilizer Science, Soil Science, Plant Physiology, and General Geology; (15) Plant Pathology, with additional exams in Crop Science, Mycology, Botany, Plant Physiology, and Plant Pathology; (16) Veterinary Medicine, with additional exams in Animal Physiology, Histology, Animal Pathology, Animal Anatomy, and Bacteriology and Immunology; (17) Statistics Group A, with additional exams in Demography, Labor Studies, Calculus, Sociological Theory, Statistics, and Urban and Rural Sociology; (18) Statistics Group B, with additional exams in Calculus, Statistics, Accounting, Finance, Monetary Banking, and Economic Theory; (19) International Finance and Trade, with additional exams in Finance, Monetary Banking, Economic Theory, Accounting, Statistics, International Trade and Exchange, and Modern European and American Economic History; (20) Public Administration, with additional exams in Municipal Administration, Finance, Public Administration, Chinese History, Political Systems, Modern European and American History, and Western Political Thought.

Chinese Science Society Held Annual Meeting Preparatory Meeting Yesterday 190

Organizing Two Committees for Health and Entertainment

Decided to Conduct Group Inspections After the Closing of the Annual Meeting

The 18th annual meeting of the Chinese Science Society is scheduled to be held in Chongqing, Sichuan and the Jialing River Hot Spring Park for seven days starting on August 17th. On August 5th, the Minsheng Industrial Company will send a special ship to Shanghai to pick up the members. All the details were reported in the previous newspaper. At 6:00 pm the day before yesterday (28th), the society held a preparatory meeting for the annual meeting to discuss health, entertainment, order, and other matters. The following is a record:

The preparatory meeting was attended by more than 30 people, including Lu Zuofu, Hu Gangfu, Ding Xuanfu, He Dekui, Tang Bo, Ge Chenghui, Yang Yunzhong, and Li Zhenpian. The chairman was Yang Yunzhong. The matters discussed were: (1) The cabin space is not enough, so it was decided to decorate the economy cabin to accommodate the members; (2) The special ship is the Min Gui, which is docked at the Zhaoshang North Bund. When boarding, contact the Zhaoshang Puan Ship Reception Office at the North Bund; (3) After arriving in Hankou, visit Wuhan University; (4) Yichang, Wanxian, and Kui Fu all made special stops for shore excursions; (5) Li Zhenpian, Ge Chenghui, Zhang Xiangwen, Zhu Changya, and Ye Shanding were appointed as members of the Health Committee, and major pharmacies and hospitals in the city will provide medicines. The committee will supervise the food and all health matters on board; (6) He Dekui, Yang Yunzhong, Zhou Rongxian, and Hu Gangfu were appointed as members of the Entertainment Committee to prepare for all entertainment matters on board, and musicians attending the meeting were asked to bring various musical instruments.

Annual Meeting Papers: The following annual meeting papers have been received from Shanghai: (1) Research on Yellow Grout in Sichuan Province (Hu Ze); (2) Records of Sichuan Frogs and Snakes; (3) New Genus of Cyprinidae in West China (Fang Bingwen); (4) Records of Animals in the Lower Reaches of the Yangtze River (Bing Zhi); (5) New Species of Sand Shell Weaving Worm (Ni Dashu); (6) New Species of Zhejiang Salamander (Zhang Mengwen); (7) Distribution of the Tree Genus in China (Qian Chongshu Fang Wenpei); (8) Records of Nanjing Plants (Pei Jian); (9) Blue-Green Algae in Nanjing (Wang Zhijia); (10) Records of Chinese Hemlock (Zheng Wanjun); (11) Nanjing Leaf Feet (Xu Fengzao); (12) Behavior of Goldfish During Reproduction (He Xirui). There are also 10 chemical papers on Chi Yu-li, Tian Yu-lin, Ma Ji-ming, Miao Ji-sheng, and Li Yong-mao.

Group Inspection: Sichuan has always been known as the Land of Abundance, with abundant products for scientific research, such as the use of the Dujiangyan water conservancy project for power generation, the salt of Zigong and Wutongqiao, the paper of Jiajiang and Dazhu, the bamboo shoots of Xufu, the wine of Luzhou, the silver ear of northern Sichuan, the summer cloth of Yingchang, and the silk of Jiading, as well as rice, wheat, soybeans, medicinal herbs, etc., which can be used by several southwestern provinces. Coal, iron, and oil are everywhere. There are many species of animals and plants, and Europeans and Americans come to collect them in an endless stream. The Institute of Biology of the Society has also sent people to Sichuan for collection in recent years, and new genera and species have been discovered from time to time. The important goal of the Society's annual meeting in Sichuan this year is to collect and inspect. After the closing of the annual meeting, they will go to Qingshan, Mount Emei, and Zigong for inspection in three groups: (1) inspecting geology; (2) collecting specimens; (3) investigating industry. Therefore, this year's annual meeting will not only make contributions to science, but also greatly benefit people's livelihood.

The Director of the Hunan Provincial Library Came to Shanghai to Investigate 191

The Hunan Provincial Zhongshan Library was destroyed in 1918. All the old books were burned. In July 1920, the Hunan Provincial Government decided to restore it as soon as possible and appointed Huang Ji as the director of the library to actively carry out the work. Mr. Huang rebuilt the buildings and purchased books, with the goal of restoring the library to its former glory in one year. More than 20,000 types of books, nearly 200,000 volumes, were purchased. The library was officially opened in September 1920, with five departments: general reading, special reading, children's reading, magazine reading, and newspaper reading. In order to expand the library and improve the classification and numbering of books, Director Huang came to Shanghai and Ningbo to investigate and discussed in detail with Huang Jingwan, Wu Yanren, Tao Zhixing, Du Dingyou, Gui Zhibai, Liu Guojun, and Jiang Kanghu. It is heard that Mr. Huang will visit the Zhejiang Provincial Library in Hangzhou for a few days before returning to Hunan.

Situation at Shanghai Business College Heard Yesterday 194

Ministry of Education Cables, Appoints Professor Zhen He

Professor Jiang Xiangqing Recounts His Service

(Central News Agency, Nanjing, 29th) The Ministry of Education has learned from news reports that Shanghai Business College has already appointed professors for the coming year. This matter should first be verified and approved by the Ministry. On the 29th, a cable was sent to the college inquiring whether this was true.

It is further reported that students at the National Shanghai Business College, due to the failure to achieve their goal of restoring the Central University's Business School (i.e., restoring the Business School of Central University), have caused a disturbance. The Ministry of Education is sending Section Chief Xie Shuying to Shanghai to investigate (before the general examination).

After Xie's arrival, some people pointed out issues with the college's operations, including the salary of Professor Jiang Xiangqing, alleging that Jiang's salary suddenly increased from 120 yuan to 240 yuan, an act of favoritism. According to Jiang, such remarks are akin to veiled slander. Originally, he held a concurrent position, but due to repeated requests from students and the president, he agreed to become a full-time professor starting last semester, to meet the expectations of the school and students. Having switched to a full-time position, he naturally deserves the treatment of a full-time professor. As for the so-called "favoritism," he does not know what it refers to. Before serving at the Business College, he had little or no contact with the several presidents who had come and gone, nor with any of the college's professors or students. This is a demonstrable fact. The students' request for him to become full-time began last summer. At that time, he was unable to leave his teaching position at another school. By last winter, the student union submitted a request to the school authorities for a full-time appointment letter and dispatched representatives twice for further negotiations. He reluctantly resigned from his other school position and became a full-time professor at the Business College. The student union's request and the two announcements from the student union in the college magazine are recorded below:

Letter from the Student Union to Jiang Xiangqing: Dear Mr. Xiangqing, since your arrival at our school, your rich experience and enthusiastic guidance have revitalized the stagnant athletic atmosphere of our school. In addition to being grateful and inspired, the students humbly request that you serve as a full-time professor at our school next semester, so that our students can benefit and learn more in their studies and cultivation. In addition to submitting a separate request to the school authorities, we hereby send this special letter of request, respectfully praying for your generous agreement. With best regards, (Seal of the National Shanghai Business College Student Union)

January 6, 1933

Announcement from the Student Union: The announcement from the student union in the 97th issue of the college magazine states: "The students of our college are diligent and studious, and have always been praised by people in society, and are particularly interested in sports. The authorities are also strongly advocating it in order to cultivate healthy and promising youth. Since the arrival of athletic expert Mr. Jiang Xiangqing to serve as a guide, the results have been steadily improving for several years. This semester, we are working even harder, and various ball teams have been established one after another. The external competitions and internal practices are very popular for a time. However, Mr. Jiang is very busy with official duties and also serves as a professor at other schools. His guidance to our college is also of a concurrent nature, so he cannot be a full-time mentor. The students are all deeply regretful. In the past, President Xu and the students have repeatedly requested Mr. Jiang to come to the college full-time, so that he can study with the students day and night and develop the college's sports to the best possible level. Later, due to the resolute retention of other schools, it was not possible. Recently, we reiterated the previous request and expressed our sincere desire to Mr. Jiang, asking him to do his best to decline the teaching position at other schools and serve full-time at our college. It is heard that Mr. Jiang is unable to refuse the enthusiasm of the faculty and students of our college and has agreed. If so, the development of sports in our college from next semester can be imagined. It is hoped that Mr. Jiang will certainly accept this sincere request and strive to realize it, which is what the faculty and students of our college are looking forward to." Jiang's spirit of sportsmanship: Jiang is known for his loyalty and straightforwardness. He has always held a "stay if we agree, leave if we don't" attitude. According to him, he has returned the appointment letter for the 22nd year (i.e., from August 1st to July 31st of the following year) to the college. From August 1st, he will not ask or care about anything related to the college. He also said that he usually gets along well with his colleagues and students. This time, due to the student unrest, he wanted to avoid getting involved in the vortex because he also held the position of student affairs director (i.e., moral education), but he was not allowed by the facts. Therefore, he did not hesitate to speak earnestly and repeatedly to the students to fulfill his duties of influencing and guiding them. When persuasion was ineffective and advice was not heeded, he continued to stop them. As a result, he, who was once welcomed by the students, is now resented by them. At the same time, two or three colleagues on the other side, who were usually friendly, have now, due to the student unrest, developed differences or even become enemies because of their different views and opinions. Speaking of this, he is heartbroken, and thinking of it, he is painful. In short, because of the student unrest, he sold his friends and made enemies. Everything in the past is unbearable to look back on. He is by nature responsible, which has caused him pain. Clever people ridicule him as a relic of the times. He said that since the times are like this, he can only accept it. He finally said, "I am a sportsman. Although I absolutely do not admit that the past actions were inappropriate, in order to comply with the sportsmanship and creed of 'be a good loser', I have decided to resign, which is to show my sportsmanship."

New Atmosphere at Gaoqiao Seaside Bathing Beach 198

Since the Gaoqiao Seaside Hotel has been built, it has strived for perfection in all necessary facilities. In the past, the road from the hotel to the beach was full of sand, mud, bricks, and stones, making it difficult to walk. Now, zongdan is laid to the beach, so there is no longer any discomfort to the feet. The shower room has been installed, so you can avoid the discomfort of dirtiness after sea bathing. The scale column is erected to indicate the depth of the water, and there is a lifeboat available, so there is no danger. Therefore, the atmosphere has been renewed. The sea breeze is cool, and you can watch the sunrise and sunset, and the moonrise over the horizon. The beautiful scenery and good times are indeed the only holy place for outdoor life to escape the summer heat. There is a special room for members of the Chinese Swimming Research Association, with special treatment.

"Physical Education Teaching Method" Published 202

Physical Education Teaching Method, compiled by physical education expert Wu Yunrui, is divided into two parts: the upper part is a general discussion, discussing learning psychology, textbook compilation, and organization of procedures, etc., based on educational psychology, the teaching propositions of the Sanderson school, and the author's teaching experience. The lower part discusses the practical teaching methods of gymnastics, games, ball games, track and field, swimming, etc., based on the author's ten years of self-study and teaching experience. The materials in the entire book are practical and cannot be compared with empty talk about principles. The exquisite printing and low price are also the characteristics of this book. The actual price per copy is 9 jiao, and the postage is 1 jiao 2 fen. It is sold by Qin Fen Bookstore on Fourth Horse Road.

Davis Cup Challenge Round, First Day

British Momentum Strong, Winning Two Singles Matches in a Row 203

Austin Takes the Lead, Straight Sets Victory Over Merlin

Penley Defeats Cochet 3-2, A Hard-Earned Victory

Yesterday's Doubles Match, France Wins the First Set 6-3 204

(Havas News Agency, Paris, 28th) The Davis Cup Challenge Round between Britain and France began today. As a result of the first day, Britain won three singles matches in a row, taking a great advantage with a score of 2-0.

(1) Austin (UK) (6-3, 6-4, 6-0) Merlin (France)

(2) Penley (UK) (8-10, 6-4, 8-6, 3-6, 6-1) Cochet (France)

The Grand Occasion of the Challenge Round 205

Before noon today, the ticket office of the Roland Garros tennis court was crowded with people. By 11:00, the tickets had been sold out. Those who arrived later, in the hope of entering, tried to break into the court, but were turned back by a large group of police officers. At 1:00 PM, the venue was packed. At 2:20, President Lebrun entered the venue and was warmly welcomed by the audience. At 2:47, Merlin served, and the first singles match between Britain and France began.

Austin First Wins Over Merlin 206

First Set, First Game, Merlin won, in an easier manner, but afterwards the competition became more intense, and Austin's skills gradually became more obvious, but Merlin also worked hard to resist. Austin won four games in a row, making it 4-1, then 4-2, 5-2, Merlin regained a game, making it 5-3, but Austin finally won 6-3.

Second Set, Austin won four games in a row, Merlin worked hard to counterattack, making it 4-4 tie, but Austin won two more games in a row and won 6-4.

Third Set, Austin won three games in a row, and after a fierce competition in the fourth game, Austin still won 6-0. Although Merlin lost, his ability to make Austin feel that he was not easy to deal with in his first international competition with a master Austin is commendable.

Penley Also Defeats Cochet 207

First Set, in the second match, Cochet was wearing shorts, while Penley was wearing long trousers, which was quite interesting. When the two entered the venue, more than 15,000 spectators gave them a warm welcome. At the beginning of the match, Cochet made Penley run around tiredly, but Penley tried his best to resist. His skills are noteworthy. Cochet once took a 4-1 lead, but Penley made it 4-4 tie. The two sides then won four games each, making it 8-8. Then Cochet, like a horse out of rein, could no longer be controlled and won two games in a row, winning the first set 10-8.

Second Set, Cochet once took a 4-2 lead, but Penley won four games in a row and won 6-4 instead.

Third Set, the competition situation was still fierce. If one of the two temporarily took the lead, the other would immediately counterattack and make it a tie. Penley once took a 6-5 lead, and only needed to win one more ball to win the third set, but Cochet made it 6-6. However, Penley finally won two more games in a row and won 8-6.

Fourth Set, after the break, the match continued. Penley, seeing that he could win the match if he won another set, tried hard to make Cochet submit. Penley once had a 3-1 lead. At this point, Cochet went to the net to intercept and won five games in a row, winning 6-3.

Fifth Set, Penley had a clear advantage, and Cochet, exhausted, had difficulty coping. Penley won five games first, and Cochet regained one game, but Penley finally won 6-1.

(Havas News Agency, Paris, 29th) The Davis Cup Challenge Round doubles match was almost postponed due to the rain at first, but it still started at 4:00 PM in the afternoon. There were many spectators. The British team players have been changed. Penley will be replaced by Lee. The French team won the first set 6-3.
